To the Oak Ridge Institute of Nuclear Studies




12 January 1951




Gentlemen:




One of our physicians, Dr. H. Lee Wylie, has already sent application for enrollment in your four-weeks course on the handling of radioisotopes.




Please do not act on this application. It has become obsolete with the first results we obtained in the prosecution of the ORANUR Project. The reaction of orgone energy to nuclear energy (1 mg radium) was so extreme and penetrating that any kind of attempt at protection in the usual routine sense became meaningless. Healthy mice became sick at 50 feet distance from 1 mg. radium which was shielded by ½” lead and deposited in a 20 fold accumulator

*

 within a metal-lined orgone room. Three experimenting observers developed nausea, dizziness, cramps in diaphragm, parasthesias and conjunctivitis 50 to 200 feet 

outside

 the experimental hall in the free fresh air. 

The entire laboratory building has become unusable with no radium in it

. We omit other most peculiar reactions.




It is the orgone energy which penetrates everything, including lead and cement walls. It is the orgone energy which reacted so violently to the radium. Therefore, no protection by lead bricks, long handling tongs, lead aprons or masks and similar measures can be taken in our type of work. We are proceeding with our experiments for further results. We are informing you on the results so far in order to explain why it became meaningless to send physicians for training in protective health measures until we have learned more about the new phenomena. Furthermore, we wish to have these facts on record with the AEC.




We do not know where we are going but we are definitely on our way at a breathtaking tempo.




Sincerely yours,

 (signed) Simeon J. Tropp, M.D.

To the Radioisotopes Division, Atomic Energy Commission




19 January 1951




Gentlemen:




Subject: Application No. 8226




The scientific workers at Orgonon have all fully recovered from the blow which was reported in our letter of January 12, 1951, to judge from the positive changes in the blood pictures and general wellbeing. We are continuing with our experiments.




The stormy events of the past two weeks have overthrown our whole plan of experimentation as outlined in our application No. 8226. We are forced by the results to rearrange our procedures. The severe reaction of orgone energy to nuclear energy, observed in the use of only 1 milligram radium, has, of course, precluded the use of from 4 to 20 millicuries of P-32. Still, it is of crucial importance to test the OR energy in reaction to radioisotope 

solutions

. This, we believe, must now be done on a much smaller scale in order to avoid a repetition of the fierceness of the OR energy reactions. We believe that about 10 

microcuries

 of P-32 would suffice to obtain unequivocal results.




As we reported before, any attempt at protection against OR energy reaction is completely out of the question. Since OR energy experimentation is far outside all routine measures, we are forced to take the risks involved. During this week, our laboratory building was still unusable, but it too has calmed down considerably. The few microcuries of P-32 would not be used as previously planned for the injection of mice; we would only put it into our 20 fold orgone energy charger which is located within a strong orgone energy room. P-32 would only be exposed to OR energy for about ½ hour daily for a period of three days, as we have done formerly with one milligram radium.




Would it now be possible to change our application No. 8226 to the procurement of only 10 microcuries of P-32 solution? Please advise us as to this possibility. We shall keep you regularly informed on all major developments and would appreciate your further kind cooperation.




We are sill planning on obtaining the help of the field service of the AEC at a later date. We cannot yet foresee in what manner this service could assist us at the present stage of NR plus OR experimentation.




We are preparing a complete report on the results obtained so far which will be sent to you in due time.




Sincerely yours,

 Simeon J. Tropp, M.D.

I discovered through Eva PAINTING

1 February 1951




I continue painting. This is a very great experience. The pleasure to let color composition stream out of one’s fingers is something very exciting. There is usually only a core of an idea. Around this core the colors and forms group themselves 

quite on their own

. This is true self-regulation.




Last night, from 1 to 5 a.m., I painted very slowly, pleasantly and carefully a young girl resting on a meadow under a tree. It was very great and deep.




Perspective comes about by itself as it were. Depths and shading, too. There is an 

urge

 to paint, even against distractions or intentions to the contrary.




I found a new way of expression. I have no one to talk to. I do not express myself, as I did twenty years ago, in lectures. I no longer enjoy the acclaim of an audience. Writing of books and articles, good as they may be, are more duty than pleasure. I do not have any social stimulation. Most people around me are helpers, often nuisance admirers whom I have to train into being workers. Mickey

*

 comes closest to being up to my level of thinking. Thus I live in lonesomeness.




8 February 1951




Once again I am turning to my diary, my old, good friend, patient and taking it all. I am being discovered by the public at large, with respect and humbleness. Inquiries for lectures, papers, contributions to discussions are coming in at an increasing rate. My books are flowing out into all corners of the world. They still cling to “psychology” of 1930—but they cling. They have not yet discovered the infant, but they soon will. They still call it “personality.”




I am painting one picture after another. I discovered a new way of expression, a good way, a way of 

seeing

. I paint from memory, from what I have seen over the years. The Orgone did not yet come through fully. It will, in due time.




I am waiting for SPRING.




11 February 1951

 4 a.m.




I am busy correcting some spots in pictures of a few weeks ago. Here are some of the things important enough to be written down.







Painting came upon me, or, rather, began to pour out of myself, quite unexpectedly but also quite logically: I am a 

“visual”

 type. Everything goes into me and out of me through the eyes. My girls used to tell me that my eyes were “dangerous.” My discoveries of the formal expression is essentially an eye problem. I love to look at things, to let them sink in, as it were.




Eyes and hands, especially fingers, unite and “it pours” from them when I paint. Somehow, memories of landscapes seen and traveled through long ago, are still alive without special sharpness. These images emerge with formation of shapes and harmonic integration of color. I am of course no learned artist but I feel I 

can

 do it. The formation of the “ancestors” for instance was nearly quite without participation of thought. I let the forms just stream out. It is what MacDonald

*

 the other day called “

my charm—

” Charm, bewitchment; great human powers, killed in every child at birth.




I discovered some days ago the 

Spectral display

 with Vacor flashes. Now, LIGHT has come to mean so much. The old quarrel between the Newtonians and the Goethe admirers about the function of light. The urge to study colors and light, as it arises from dawn and sinks into dusk, is great. Daylight is clearly a function of high pulse frequency and rapid birth and death of OR units. The scale develops 

upwards

 from the night blue over purple (in shades) toward blue (dark), blue (light) to all shades of “white” light. Light is not really white. There is no proper name for the color of white light. The appearance of a rainbow is a riddle. The grating by rain is only the mechanics of it. It has something to do with discharges, since discharges go with spectral breakup.




Emotionally, painting became a major experience. I am discovering my “seeing,” so to speak. I can find out now what I see 

true

 and what 

false

, and whether I see things correctly at all. And I love to paint. It is something so visible.




I must inevitably, think of Leonardo da Vinci. It occurred to me today that he too had combined art and science. He too tried so many things.




Somehow, Eva has repaid me for my long suffering for her by having given me the painting outfit.




Painting of Orgone phenomena will, if I acquire the technical skill, save me a lot of writing.

To H. E. Macdonald




9 April 1951




Dear Dr. MacDonald,




I have just read the letter you received from Dr. Adams of Bryn Mawr College. It is good that scientists sit down and start doing experiments instead of merely talking about it. However, I am obliged to prevent possible disaster, and to do some preventative medicine. The following points are essential to rational scientific conduct in matters of biogenesis. It has been our policy for more than a decade now, to adhere to the following rules set down and to be followed by anyone who attempts to form an opinion on orgonomic biogenetic problems:







We are not out for any confirmation of any of our experiments; we do not care whether anyone confirms our experiments or not. We do not recognize any authorities whatsoever in the realm of orgonomic research, except those who have proven to our satisfaction that they have studied the subject carefully and have submitted to the full scrutiny of their emotional, structural and scientific ability to form valid opinions in our realm of work.




Every single experiment that is being repeated by any one must under no circumstances be separated or isolated from the total experiential, experimental, and methodical as well as theoretical framework within which the single experiment has grown and can find its proper evaluation. For example, Experiment XX cannot be done without knowledge of the physical orgone energy functions in the living organism and in the atmosphere. It is completely useless to look at a single screw from an airplane and to strut around with opinions about that screw without knowing exactly 

that

 it belongs to an airplane and 

where

 it belongs.




Every experiment must be done according to the description and the rules of orgonomy. In experiment XX, for example, freezing, continuous observation over a period of 5 to 10 years in sterile condition, and comparative studies with other biogenetic phenomena such as disintegration and decay of organic tissue, etc., are of crucial importance. Exact reports on the procedures followed, must be submitted for any discussion of the results.




Since there are no authorities whatsoever in this new realm of natural science, it is required that the one who does the experiment proves to our satisfaction that he has studied the total subject carefully. No experiment makes sense without having used an orgone energy accumulator, having seen the orgone energy in the dark in the orgone energy room, and having observed the many manifestations which have been published in our literature.




Most essential of all, perhaps, is careful observation of the emotional involvements which go with any work connected with life energy. It isn’t true that our scientists are objective, on the contrary, they are mostly gravely prejudiced or steeped in mechanistic, chemistic, atomistic and other ideas which are, by mere logic, secondary to the orgone energy functions which are of a primordial nature and 

BASIC

 to any understanding of all other functions. 

One cannot judge orgonomy from the standpoint of bacteriological functions, just as one cannot judge an airplane from an isolated screw. It is the other way around, A staphylococcus must be judged from the standpoint of orgone energy vesicles

. One cannot judge cosmic orgone energy from the standpoint of static electricity. One cannot judge the problem of bio-energy from the standpoint of a single love affair, but the other way around. And last, but not least, one must be well acquainted with the emotional, religious prejudices and the structural anxieties which have so far and so successfully prevented a rational approach to the problem of biogenesis. It is out of the question that a repetition take place of the Bastian—Pasteur misery.

*

 Catholic inspired and religiously prescribed ideas are blocking the way to any such inquiry, and they must be acknowledged and removed first.







Since no air germs of any protozoa have ever been found and demonstrated in the air, and since, furthermore, the whole air germ theory is pure myth, kept up ad hoc in order to prevent the knowledge of biogenesis, the proof as to the existence of air germs of cancer cells, colpidia, protozoa of any kind rests squarely on the shoulders of those who adhere to it. Our proofs of biogenesis are abundant. We shall not partake in any discussion whatsoever on air infection unless its representatives demonstrate the origin of protozoa in the air.




Such grave matters cannot be decided by debate Pro and Con. They can only be decided by practical observation and experience. i.e. by using orgone energy accumulators, by looking into microscopes for years on end and by doing all the things empirically which are crucial to the formation of any valid scientific opinion.




This is the scope of the discovery of the orgone energy. And it requires full adjustment of anyone who tries to form a valid opinion about it. The responsibilities involved are grave and concern life and death of millions of people. Please, do not forget this for a single moment and convey this idea if you can to everyone who comes near orgonomy.

To Wesley Knapp




August 9

th

, 1951




Dear Mr. Knapp:




I received your letter of July 23rd. It interested me rather much since it posed some of the same problems which I met head-on when I started out, 24 years ago, with mental hygiene work in Austria. There can be no doubt about the necessity of having orgonomic knowledge spread among the people in an easily understandable manner. It would be a matter of course to do so. However, the dangers of such a procedure are enormous and perilous as everyone, including myself, has learned the hard way, who followed the basically logical line of thinking. What one is apt to overlook is the deep fear of the living and the severe biopathic structure in the majority of people which makes it impossible for them to follow up what appears to their reason logical and self-evident. Pornographic degeneration and distortion of sex-economy

*

 is the first grave threat to be mastered. There would be no greater danger to a future efficiency of orgonomic knowledge in a new type of education in infants and adolescents, than to proceed without having full control over the inclination to distort sex-economic knowledge into pornographic channels. The other danger is, according to past experiences, that the factual, medical and educational tasks are not tackled practically step by step in a skilled way, but that an ideology is build, according to other political ideologies which make a lot of noise, promise heaven on earth, overlook the tremendous disease which harasses the human race and is bound to fail at the first real obstacle to be overcome.




The severity of the task is not of my making, but is given in the circumstances under which the masses of people have lived for such a long time. You can rest assured that no day passes by without uttermost efforts to cope with the problem you have posed in your letter.




There would be no greater disaster for humanity than a distorted sex-economy, in the vein of past distortions of crucial teachings. The lesson learned in Russia should be a warning to anyone who feels that new ideas should be put on a mass basis.




May I have your permission to possibly publish your letter in one of the coming Orgone Energy Bulletins, together with my answer on an enlarged basis?

The basic problem however is not more writing, but making already written stuff practically effective in people. How to get people moving.




The psychoanalytic world assumes the spite is due to unconscious repressed wishes. It believes that the remedy is to make the repressed conscious. This, of course, fails since the spite (“I won’t”) is a symptom and expression of structure (“I can’t”), unapproachable by ideas alone.




The orgonomic view holds the lethargy to be an expression of the immobilization of the organism due to chronic armoring. No conscious drill, nor making ideas conscious can move the massive blocking of will and action. It is, to this view, necessary to break the biological blocking to get life energy, and, with it, will and action streaming again. However, the basic structure, so tells us our medical experience, is unchangeable. The focus of attention therefore must be centered upon the new generations yet to be born, and prevention of emotional blocking right from the beginning.




There orgonomy is the most revolutionary approach to the nature of man. It reaches deepest, beyond the conscious and unconscious into man’s biological existence.

14 January 1952




I feel Life pulsing again fully, strongly, unbeatably. Things are happening fast:




While I was preparing the Listings of the archive material for the WR-History of Orgonomy Biography, an ad appeared in the 

Psychiatric Quarterly

 calling all who knew Freud to contribute letters, reports, works to his Archives to be established in the Library of Congress. I have plenty to give here, alright, but will they want it, really?




They wrote very nice, friendly, humble letters, expressing satisfaction over my, our, collaboration. But will they like it.




Involved are peoples’ highly private affairs, love affairs, cheat affairs, and other affairs; Freud’s personal tragedy, scientific tragedy, historic tragedy, his hopes in me and his later disappointment since my work made a turn he feared. Involved are, too, the fates of future generations of newborn infants, whether they should grow the 

sublimating way

natural self-regulation

Can I trust them better than I did 1934 when they all took me for a ride at Luzern,

*

 nobody being aware at all of what was going on. We shall see. But careful procedure is essential and perfect frankness as usual, my “devastating” bluntness. What a wonderful weapon 

if

Oranur is still going on. Some people suffer much, but it works its way through the organism, breaking blockings, causing movements, driving evil latent symptoms to the surface, then healing them. What a possibility! To use Oranur against emotional, bioenergetic diseases—successfully.




I know I must keep several of my basic life lines going if I am to proceed further:




First, I must not ever permit my bioenergetic system to go stale or sluggish or filled with DOR

*

 from stasis of Life Energy, out of false considerations which don’t mean a thing and are obsolete in a few months. I must live my love the right way, not the wrong way as I did most of the time.




Second, I must further sharpen my weapon of using the truth wisely and bluntly, sharpen it by further experience in practical use, by making not too big mistakes or irreparable ones, as for instance keeping my light too long under the bushel.




Third, I must not ever abandon Peter who needs me. I would suffer from it more than he would, but to guide this boy through puberty, through all the pitfalls of a crazy world is crucial to me and to him.




Fourth, I must let myself go freely in the new contacts which will come my way over the coming years, freely, honestly, without lament or false aspirations. I just must keep my old good ways going through all of it. My way proved usually the right one even if after years only. Why not repay some of the confidence my way of life had in me. The hardest thing, though, is to keep one’s way going by not permitting every day petty human affairs to slowly infringe on it, undermine it invisibly, rendering me helpless without awareness. Keep other ways in respect but at some distance.

It’s a professional job. The fact that the emotional problem of human living was some thousands of years ago entangled with religion must not obfuscate its true nature, which is, truly, engineering of the human character structure.




Peter put his head yesterday to my shoulder while I worked in the Lab and complained bitterly that he can scarcely think of anything but girls. I told him, it will become worse still in the coming years, until he will find a girl he can love.




Greta Hoff just told me they are wrestling desperately in Maine social agencies with the genitality problem in adolescents.

In the spring of 1952, knowledge that in orgone energy the stronger system attracts and draws energy from the weaker system (the reversed orgonomic potential), and that orgone is absorbed by water, played a critical role in Reich’s development of a new experimental tool: the cloudbuster. Designed initially in an effort to remove or weaken heavy dark clouds that hovered over Orgonon during the Oranur experiment, hollow metal pipes mounted on a heavy metal base and grounded through empty BX cables in a well or lake were elevated to draw energy slowly and in small amounts from the atmosphere and to the more highly charged earth. Affecting changes in orgone energy concentrations in the atmosphere made it possible to influence weather and other atmospheric phenomena.




Draft of a Letter to the Surgeon General of the United States




29 April 1952




Dear Sir:




I am referring to the First Report on the Oranur Experiment which was sent to you sometime in October 1951. This letter is being written after an inspection tour which I undertook on April 22nd and 23rd, 1952 in a circle of about 250 miles around this region. The purpose of this inspection was to see how far the Oranur effects have spread.




It was found that high counts (up to 600 CPM) and down to normal again were prevalent in a region of a diameter of about 40 to 50 miles, reaching West to Berlin, New Hampshire and East to some 10 miles west of Farmington, Maine.




The functions and phenomena involved are too complicated and also too new to be comprehensibly presented at this point. However, the following may not require elaborate proof.




As reported in the first Oranur Report, Oranur effects manifest themselves first in an elicitation of latent or past diseases. Several hundred mice died among other things with signs of asphyxiation. There is little danger involved, as long as people who are under Oranur effect follow certain rules, such as much fresh air through ventilation, being outdoors, frequent baths, and, if possible, from time to time removal to a region where the atmospheric orgone energy is normal, in cases of severe over irradiation.




This institution has no apparatus to inform the population in this vicinity, and should the Oranur effects spread further, to inform the population farther away of the necessary measures to avoid hardships and danger to health. We therefore request the cooperation of the United States Health Agencies, to give to the public well in advance the proper information regarding the means of countering ill effects of atmospheric Oranur pressure. This can easily be done and should not be postponed unnecessarily, since it is still highly uncertain what an extended, severe atmospheric Oranur pressure can do. Continuous tests are being conducted at Orgonon, where several buildings have become uninhabitable and cannot be used for work. I have exposed myself to the fullest possible dose of Oranur to test a possible borderline towards severe impairment to health.




We expect your answer with eagerness.




To David H. Stevens




4 June 1952




State of Maine Health and Welfare Department




Dear Mr. Stevens:




I wish to inform you that I am succeeding in removing the dangerous DOR effects over the Rangeley region (see 

The Oranur Experiment: First Report

) by way of influencing the formation and movements of clouds. The results will be published in due time.




Would you be kind enough to forward the enclosed carbon copy of this letter to the appropriate agency of the Federal Health service?




To Commissioner of Patents




28 June 1952




Dear Sir:




This letter is to inform your office, in a preliminary way and in order to secure my scientific priority, of the following two technological discoveries made in my laboratory at Orgonon, Rangeley, Maine, during the past 18 months approximately:




1. 

Cloudbusting




It is technically possible, by using the so-called “orgonomic potential” (potential from low to high) in primordial Orgone Energy functioning, to disperse clouds, to concentrate water vapors in the atmosphere to the extent of making rain, and to draw atmospheric energy into lakes and rivers. This also makes it possible to remove the so-called “DOR”—clouds which lately appeared over this region and caused biophysical distress to many people. It will also, basically and on principle, from now onward be technically in all probability possible, to destroy thunder clouds, and, in principle, there are no longer any obstacles in the way to influence or even destroy hurricanes (at least theoretically), to create clouds and rain over deserts, to stop or diminish the causes of floods.




This preliminary information will be extensively dealt with in publications at some future date.







2. “

Melanor

”




In the course of the Oranur Experiment, a function in the atmosphere was discovered which causes rocks of an ordinary nature to turn black and to disintegrate at a much accelerated rate. (microscopically: in a bionous fashion). The black something has been named by me: “Melanor.” It reveals all kinds of chemical and physical properties which are still under investigation; among these properties is especially one most interesting one: 

change

, and 

possibly creation of matter.




This function, too, will be extensively presented in print at some future date.

To Elsworth F. Baker, M.D.




5 August 1952




Dear Dr. Baker:




I am enclosing a few documents for your file, and for possible discussion with the lawyer.




It is of crucial importance to view clearly the situation as it is, in the 

lawful incorporation of the orgone energy into present-day social frameworks

.







It is questionable whether the orgone energy accumulator can be designated as a “device.” Are 2 palms, moved toward and against each other, or two metal plates doing the same, thus exciting orgone energy, a “device”?




Is a water jug which contains and handles water and makes drinking possible, a device in that sense?




Is a heap of steel wool which accumulates orgone energy spontaneously, a device to be inspected by the Food and Drug Administration?




Is the accumulator itself which, energetically cannot be sharply delineated from its energetic environment, a device?







I do not pretend to be able to answer these questions. The only thing I want to point out with these questions is that orgone energy devices, if at all, 

cannot possibly be delivered to the practices of the FDA as we know them.




You will see from the statements 1 and 2 that these gentlemen came with rather doubtful intentions, and that to my deep regret I had to ask them to leave Orgonon. They came fully unprepared, especially the physicist who had read only the Oranur Experiment, after we had made it clear to them in a letter of August 3rd, 1951, that 

we would cooperate with them only if they came fully prepared and familiar with the orgonomic literature

. They also did not seem to be aware of the fact that I, personally, 

have nothing whatsoever to do with the distribution of the accumulator

.




It is also quite obvious that we must work toward a new law, similar to the laws that were established to govern Radio, Television, Aeronautics, laws which will govern all matters pertaining to cosmic orgone energy engineering. Of course, I must leave the final decision as to whether an orgone energy accumulator is a device or not in the usual sense to further discussions and deliberations. Until the legal incorporation of the cosmic orgone energy in our present social law system is effectuated, and in order not to be in conflict with existent laws, I am contemplating to suggest that orgone energy accumulators be built within the respective states, and not be shipped in interstate commerce. Could you get an inquiry under way as to whether New Jersey and New York could and would under supervision of our physicians start building orgone energy accumulators for their respective states in exactly the same manner as they are built in the state of Maine? In such a case, the Food and Drug Administration would not even have the pretense of being a legal authority of the orgone energy accumulator.

5 October 1952




Today I left, I hope definitely, Ilse and Peter. I had become very ugly with her.




Characteristically, she said crying “But you need us.” Not: “We need you.”




And: “You want to make another Eva out of Peter.” Later: “I am sorry, I know Eva was her mother’s victim.”




Thus, she tries to make me bad in order to retain her self-respect.




Poor Peter—He will have to fight his way through in life. He tried desperately, as so often before, to join his mother’s and father’s hands together, not to lose them—in vain.




I left and wrote the following letter to my son:




 




My dearest Peter:




I am so very sorry that you had to witness my leaving your mother’s place this morning. She will take care of you from now on. I shall deposit money enough for you to obtain what you need for living. But soon you should pull out and learn to stand on your own feet. But, if you want to live with me now, you should do so.




Please, do not blame either mother or father for what went on. It was nobody’s fault. We just did not agree with each other any longer and we only suffered. So I feel and hope that peace will return to your home after I have left.




Now listen, Pete: I told you a few days ago that I would never leave you unless 

you want

 me to go. This morning you said I should go away. I did. But still I do not abandon or forget you. You will have to come to me when you need me. I shall be there. You will or may need me sooner or later as you grow up. You will always find me if you need me, in any way. But I shall not come to you if you do not call me.




I love you dearly and I always shall. Stay honest, straight, open minded, as you basically are. Do not follow people who hide away from the facts of life.




You can always call me at the Observatory and visit me there.




Love, Daddy

 Willy

I really know very little of nature, although I seem to know a lot more than my fellow men in this age. To my mind, science, true knowledge of our existence, has not begun yet. It was very bad fumbling so far. Think of Einstein’s terrible error.

*




Freud had just an inkling, which he soon abandoned to the psychiatrist business men.




I am bitter—yes. In the face of his own tragedy, and in the face of the tremendous problems ahead of him, man should appear more modest and less malignant than he is.




 




During the past few days I saw rocks which were battle scarred with holes, powdery, and dilapidated, smooth out very slowly on the surfaces of some.




Now this sounds perfectly crazy 

even to me

. Yet, it is true and was seen first by Tom Ross, an excellent observer of nature.




Rocks which were hurt by the ugly atomic DOR clouds and developed holes, developed “scar tissue” as does living matter. This is in itself entirely logical: The same OR energy that heals wounds in living matter 

heals decaying rock

. This is a part of the basic natural law.




27 February 1953




The “healing” of destroyed rock is just as 

incredible

 now as was the moving of bions 15 years ago. It will also be as selfevident to everyone 10 years from now as is the orgone accumulator today to those who know how it works.




The “selfevidence” is this: In wound healing a force is at work which cannot but derive from bioenergy. And bioenergy is only a function of cosmic energy, active in decaying rock.




What then is so “incredible” in “healing rocks”? Nothing but our static mind, which thinks of rocks as absolute, unchangeable beings.




To Eva Reich




4 March 1953




My dear Eva:




I have your good letter of three days ago. It seems to me you suffer from having tasted the 

bitter

 pills of life—too early, and in too heavy doses. Sadness- it certainly creates. But sadness also is a propellant in life, unexcelled. All creation stems from this kind of feel in life. Peter has it strongly; sometimes he runs away from it. But, than again, he runs away from the “usual” back to his depth. This struggle will take many many centuries.




10 March 1953




A physician, student of Orgonomy, writes the following:




“…It seems desirable to be recognized as a minority group in medicine so that we can work unmolested. Whether this recognition will in anyway be expedited by belonging to these organizations (A.M.A., American Psychiatric Association, etc.) I do not know….” This physician betrays a regrettable amount of naiveté and ignorance regarding orgonomic medicine and its status in the world. He wants to be recognized. We ask: 

by whom

? He overlooks the fact that by practicing orgonomic medicine he is operating as a pioneer whether he so wishes or not. 

He fails to recognize his own authority

. Failing to recognize 

himself

, he still expects to be recognized by 

somebody else

; more, to be recognized by the very organizations or groups which were out until recently to hamper his work or to destroy it. Imagine the radio operators of the early twenties clamoring for recognition by the telephone operators, or the electricians of the early part of the century begging the gas lamp manufacturers to recognize them. The first thing they had to do was to recognize 

themselves

 as authorities in their own field and to work toward success the hard way. To expect to “work in peace” in a world which is riddled by emotional plague actions and reactions, is to concede utter ignorance in sociology.




Orgonomy is not a branch of practical medicine, designed only to earn money with, as some medical orgonomists seem to believe. Orgonomy is a body of knowledge concerning the 

basic natural

 law, a tiny part of which falls within the realm of medicine. Whoever does not like the struggle that goes with pioneering science and medicine, would be better off in devoting his time to more peaceful tasks such as shock treatment, which is fully “recognized,” or psychoanalysis. In orgonomy, for a long time to come, hard struggle by way of writing medical reports, revues, delivering lectures, participation in public discussions, etc., will belong to the daily job of the serious worker.




To Nic Waal




17 March 1953




My dear Nic Waal

*

:




I received your inquiry and copy of your letter to Dr. Boadella. It is entirely impossible for me to pass judgment on these letters since I do not know the exact positions either of the applicant or of the teaching group. I appreciate however your frankness in keeping off the realm of physical orgone energy. I prefer your attitude by far to empty enthusiasm, but I would exempt Dr. Raknes from your criticism. Dr. Raknes has thoroughly understood the basic trends of physical orgonomy.




It is also in the interest of your students and the future physicians and teachers you train in Scandinavia, to point out that Orgonomy is 

one whole

, and that character analysis or what I once called vegeto-therapy cannot be basically and forever separated from the discovery of the life energy or organismic energy. You are dealing with physical life energy processes, or orgonotic processes, in every twitching of a muscle, in every change of vaso-vegetative equilibrium, in every orgastic discharge, and so on. I know that you know this well, but I would suggest advising your students to be at least in touch with the literature of the last 7 or 8 years concerning physical orgonomy.




It is very difficult to keep everybody informed individually on events at Orgonon. The Orgone Energy Bulletin gives a fair picture on progress in research as well as on other happenings.




In the end I would like to point out that Orgonomy is today so far spread out in the world, and studied in so many institutions that it is completely out of my hands.




I hope you are personally well.




To the Office of the Governor of Maine




13 May 1953




Gentlemen:




We wish to inform you of the following:




In April, 1952, this Institute has started experiments in atmospheric Orgone Energy control. During the drought of 1952, very cautious first steps were undertaken in this direction which resulted successfully in the construction of a machine called “Cloudbuster.” Three such Cloudbusters, constructed at the Southworth Machine Company in Portland, are at present located and operate at Orgonon, Rangeley, Maine.




We intend, during the coming summer months, to proceed further in our weather control experiments at a more advanced rate, and with greater intensity than last year. It happened already this year, as it did last year, that weather predictions by the Portland and Boston Weather Stations were upset or contradicted by our experiments. This fact may endanger aircraft pilots and also embarrass the weather stations. Therefore, we prefer to inform you of these facts. Cooperation with other agencies of the State will, we believe, become necessary in order to cope with the situation.




The tendency toward a new and severe drought this summer is clearly discernible to the Orgone Institute. Therefore, operations with the cloudbusters are concentrating on the fire danger with the aim of keeping Maine wet and green. First steps in making contact with The Forest Fire Control service in Franklin County have been taken, and we would appreciate your cooperation in furthering the coordination of the various public services concerning weather control and forest fire prevention.




A first publication on the subject is enclosed; other publications will follow.




Sincerely yours

 Orgone Institute

To William Moise

†




2 August 1953




My dear Moise:




It took so long to compile this message to you because of the week of the conference and its preparation. Since then I have had more time and could study your material.




First let me tell you that you acted, as do most able beginners in almost every human endeavor, much too eagerly. Eagerness and enthusiasm are important qualities in accomplishing things. However, they should be directed toward 

factual

 mastery of natural processes; rather than toward convincing people. I felt that you made this mistake in some of your letters to the various departments of federal and state government. These agencies of social administration are usually overburdened with work and responsibility, and also with requests from peddlers and crackpots. You did not realize fully the difference between the inquiry of the Department of Commerce and underhanded activities of unfair business competition as explained to you in my letter of July 16, 1953.




The Weather Bureau was seriously interested to learn more about our Oranur Weather Control operation (briefly—OROP). In good science one is fully entitled to argue about a new piece of knowledge. Such argument is not only rational; it is indispensable. To prove this point to yourself as a tyro in Cosmic Engineering stop now before reading further and try to answer the question: “How do I know quite positively and explainable to anyone rationally seeking answers that it was the Cloudbuster and not some coincidence that caused the raining in the east a few hours after the Ellsworth OROP?”




You will find, if you question yourself honestly, that you would not quite know how to answer this question, a question which the Weather Bureau has rightly put before you. In natural science you are not taken seriously if you are unable to tell 

how

 your result came about. This is sharply to be distinguished from the underhanded pestilent character who calls himself scientific while he tries to trip you from ambush wherever he can.




I had to work quite some time on my records to answer this question first to myself. Here it is. We can be quite certain, within the limits of still possible error, about our Ellsworth OROP for the following reasons:




1. I would have doubted the Oranur operation myself, and I would not have accepted any money,

*

 if there had been too many uncertainties in the direction of the rainfall, its layout, or the absence of well known signs of positive action. I had told Mr. Phillips, of Ellsworth, at the point of draw, when somebody wisecracked, “Now lets prepare our umbrellas.” “Don’t prepare any umbrellas yet. We can only wait and see what happens.” We do not promise any rain as we do not promise any cancer cure in ten years as some do. We simply wait and see.




2. A further mistake is the impression you gave that we were 

PROFESSIONAL

 rainmakers. 

We are no

t 

professional rainmakers

, 

not even experimental professional rainmakers

. We are busy here at Orgonon to remove the nauseating 

DOR clouds

 from our region, in order to survive our anti-nuclear research operations. It was within the framework of 

these

 DEDORIZATION operations that I hit, quite accidentally, upon the function of the 

rain

 cloud making and busting. We do not even have a well operating weather station. We have a few meteorological devices. We have no regular service in weather charting, being so few people with so may important things to do.




3. It is to us as serious workers at the roots of nature more important to know our 

failures

 than our successes. For example I tried hard to break the drought spell at the end of August and failed in making rain with the exception of two negligible short drizzles. Even this failure proved important. I learned what 

cannot

 be done as yet. This, too, secures final success if any is obtainable at all. I only succeeded in achieving some fast drifting cloud banks covering all northern Maine on Saturday, August 29, 1953, during the night. This led to an innovation: 

CONTINUOUS CLOUDBUSTING OPERATION

. This continuous operation brought fourth two new insights: First, one can remove the DOR clouds far better through continuous operation with only one or two open draw pipes; Second, in this operation somehow heavy dew appeared within about 40 miles south and west of Orgonon—a dew rich enough for the soil to appear as if drenched in rain, and for the farmer within this belt good enough not to complain about the drought. Thus the failure to obtain full blown rain on August 28th brought fourth new important facts. I still do not know 

why

 I failed this time. There was between July 15 and 23 at Orgonon (five days constant east to west OR flow 

without

 rain effect, and severe DOR). I do not 

know

 whether the drenching rains in the New York area on July 23rd was a result of this operation. They had such heavy rainfall lately in Texas. Thus you can see how crucial it is to 

know what you do not know

, always better to understand 

how you do the things you do

. Let me now tell you, also to increase your self confidence and competence as a future Oranur Weather Control operator in the face of such serious inquiries as that posed by the Weather Bureau, how I can be certain to have broken the drought in New England in the beginning of August 1952 and why I am certain of the Ellsworth draw. I expressed both of these certainties with good reason in the information I gave through you to the Bangor Daily News of July 26, 1953.




 




1. 

The Breaking of the August

, 

1952 Drought




After having tried in vain for weeks to break the drought during July, 1952 with the exception of a few rainfalls, around Orgonon, I finally hit upon an idea of predominately drawing from the direction opposite to that where you want the rain to go. I wanted the rain, as you may remember for August 1, 1952 at the bridge east of Rangeley, to go toward south in the general direction of Boston. The first rainfall occurred in 

our

 region on August 3, coming as expected from the northwest. It reached Farmington, went on to Portland reaching Boston on August 10. Here I learned that we do 

not MAKE

 rain; we only influence the OR potential in the atmosphere while we trigger the various regions of the OR envelope. Thus we judge from the time of the onset of the planned rain plus its direction our data about the trigger function of the atmospheric orgone envelope (similar but slower than radio operation), and about important criteria for self control. I claim the rain only if there are not too many uncertainties and if I know what I did and how I achieved my result.




 




2. 

The Temporary Breaking of the Drought of June-July, 1953 at Ellsworth

.




This drought had been predicted by me to the State House in Augusta, Maine, in a letter of May 13, 1953. This prediction of the drought was based on careful observation on clouds which appeared to be unable to hold together and dissipated again and again.




The Weather Bureau rightly points out that there was a weather front coming form the 

west

 at the time of this OROP. This is perfectly true. However, the Weather Bureau overlooked my report on the 

preliminary

 OROP on July 5 at Rangeley which I had made as a 

preparatory

 operation to make the result at Ellsworth the following day safer. It rained at Rangeley, coming from the west, all Monday night, July 6th as expected. This rain from the west moved to southeast as drawn and was seen in Hancock on July sixth in the afternoon as a heavy blue cloudbank to the west. The 

center

 of rain in the east, however, was at Ellsworth as stated by the various observers. It had spread past Bangor to the west to the south and east. This “Ellsworth rain,” however, was mainly caused by my drawing 

from the east

. I was at first astounded to witness the rolling in of a great front of fog and clouds many miles wide from the ocean, several hundred feet high and very dense. I had not expected the moisture to come in as it actually did from the Atlantic. It was, to my mind, basically fog and humidity from the ocean which broke the drought. You know that Eva witnessed this spectacle together with me from my car east of Hancock on the afternoon of July 6. It rained as expected and reported all through the following night with the center in Ellsworth.




The chart you drew about the course and density of the rainfall drawn from official weather reports I believe, shows clearly that its center was at Ellsworth and Bar Harbor; its direction was as intended and drawn from northwest to southeast, in accordance with the preceding OROP at Orgonon. There were 

TWO

 weather fronts, one from the west mentioned, and one from the east unmentioned in the letter of the Weather Bureau in its inquiry of the Ellsworth Experiment.




Not being a professional rainmaker and having no professional weather station at my disposal, such an assembly and coordination of facts, official and my own, is quite impressive in our favor. I would like to add, and I hope the colleagues in the Washington central Weather Bureau will take it in good humor. At times when I have leisure enough to take off from my heavier duties in experimental Oranur work, I enjoy the sudden changes which are pronounced by weather stations at the radios of Portland and Boston in accordance with our DOR removal operations. These DOR removal operations are, as I emphasized before, crucial to our continued personal as well as scientific existence at Orgonon.




These are some of the facts about the Ellsworth draw. They tell to some extent why I believe to have achieved my result at Ellsworth.




You may use this letter at your discretion in answering the letter of the Washington bureau. I have no objection to sending to the bureau a copy of this letter.




I hope Eva and you are well. I shall be in touch with you regarding the planned work at Hancock very soon.




WR




To Ivan R. Tannehill




29 October 1953




U.S. Weather Bureau




Dear Dr. Tannehill:




We refer to the experiments in the realm of Atmospheric Orgone Energy Control which have been conducted at the Orgone Institute over the past 18 months. During these operations, weather bureaus have frequently been forced to change predictions; on other occasions the forecasts became contradictory due to ORANUR Cloudbuster operations in the North East. This situation, we feel, may endanger air and sea travel.




It was, therefore, decided to file with your office reports on every ORANUR Weather Control operation which could possibly have a bearing on either sea or air travel. We do not have the facilities of nationwide communication. Should the central Weather Bureau in Washington feel that our operations should be in any way coordinated with public needs, we shall be glad to cooperate. The experiments, which are resulting also in rain-making, are basically ruled by our research activities concerning engineering of the Atmospheric Energy Envelope of the planet (CORE; Cosmic Orgone Energy Engineering). Problems of drought and desert developments are emerging from these research activities.

On 10 February 1954, the U. S. District Court for the District of Maine issued a summons in which the United States of America, plaintiff, by and through Peter Mills, U. S. attorney for the District of Maine, filed a complaint for injunction against the Wilhelm Reich Foundation, Wilhelm Reich and Ilse Ollendorff (the foundation clerk). The proceeding was brought under a section of the federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act that gives the FDA authority over shipment of medical devices in interstate commerce. Directed specifically against the orgone energy accumulator, which it claimed to be “adulterated and misbranded . . . not connected with or plugged into any source of electrical or any other type of energy or power.” It also claimed that all Reich’s writings were advertising and promotion for the accumulator. This included literature written before the discovery of orgone energy and the development of the accumulator.







WHEREFORE PLAINTIFF PRAYS that the defendants, The Wilhelm Reich Foundation, a Maine corporation, Wilhelm Reich and Ilse Ollendorff, individuals, and each and all of their officers, agents, servants, employees, attorneys, all corporations, associations, and organizations, and all persons in active concert or participation with any of them, be perpetually enjoined from directly or indirectly introducing or causing to be introduced or delivering or causing to be delivered for introduction into interstate commerce in violation of 21 U.S.C. 331 (a), any orgone energy accumulator device, in any style or model, and any and all accessories, components or parts thereof, or any similar article, in any style or model, which is misbranded within the meaning of 21 U.S.C. 352 (a) or adulterated within the meaning of 21 U.S.C. 351 (c):










AND FURTHER PRAYS:




That the aforesaid defendants, their officers, agents, servants, employees, attorneys, all corporations, associations, and organizations, and all persons in active concert or participation with any of them, be perpetually enjoined from directly or indirectly doing or causing to be done any act whether oral, written, or otherwise in the manner aforesaid or in any other manner, with respect to any orgone energy accumulator device, in any style or model, or with respect to any similar article or device while held for sale after shipment in interstate commerce, in violation of 21 U.S.C. 331 (k), which results in said article being misbranded within the meaning of 21 U.S.C. 352 (a), or adulterated within the meaning of 21 U.S.C. 351 (c):










ANY FURTHER PRAYS:




That the plaintiff be given judgment of its costs herein and for such other and further relief as to the Court may seem just and proper.




Peter Mills

 United States Attorney

To United States District Attorney Peter Mills




No date




Federal Court House, Portland, Maine




Your summons was served upon the Foundation, myself and the clerk of the Foundation, Ilse Ollendorff by your office to appear as defendants in court within 20 days. The accusation is served by the Food and Drug Administration, and the charge is fraud in matter of the discovery of the Life Energy.




I have nothing to add to the thousand of pages of evidence which has been published ever since 1936. I do not believe that matters of scientific inquiry can be decided in court; and less so, since those who challenge this discovery are corrupt conspirators of pharmaceutic business who are using, or rather abusing an agency of the United States Government to serve their own evil ends.




I wish to inform you who several years ago has helped so much in establishing this Foundation, and who knows the founders of the foundation well, I wish to inform you that having done my duty as a scientist and a citizen far beyond obligation, and having had no material gain but rather had suffered great sacrifices for this discovery, I refuse to be dragged as a “defendant” through the courts of the United States in a case of alleged fraud. I am not going to fight against corrupt business practices in court. Our organization will be dissolved to the detriment of the interest of the people, as requested. The discovery of the Life Energy is far out everywhere on this globe and it can take care of itself. I have nothing more to add to it.




Should any court find that the discovery of the Life Energy is a fraud, the world will certainly know better. There is nothing that can kill it. The evidence in the form of original documents of the corrupt and crookish nature of those keeping behind the scenes in this matter is at hand and at your disposal here at Orgonon.

. Ignore everything.

3. 

Consent Decree

.




AR I would have to make a court appearance for a consent decree. A consent decree amounts to this: We accept their injunction. I am present when the final injunction is written. I can help word it, and when it is done I can tell you exactly just what you can and cannot do.

AR thinks that both parties in this case are bona fide, honest searchers after truth. 

They

To Asa Richardson




Undated




Dear Mr. Richardson




I appreciate very much the legal help you are rendering in keeping ignorant intruders and disturbers of the peace at bay. I may in a few sentences summarize the situation; you are free to choose from this summary whatever may be useful in setting straight the facts underlying the case:




1. In 1945, with the publication of Exp. XX I predicted that the Cosmic OR energy will one day find itself in a battle against the atomic energy after matter. Otherwise it would be incomprehensible how a multibillion dollar atomic chemistry business could become so frightened of the sale of 2400 dollars worth of OR energy devices for non-medical use in a year. The fight between atomic, pharmaceutic and preatomic, cosmic OR energy is on.




2. I believe that battles of scientific beliefs cannot be fought in court or be rationally decided in court action.




3. I suggest that the battle of preatomic, massfree, Cosmic OR energy against atomic pharmaceutic interests be removed from court and be transferred to where it belongs and where it is already present, in scientific and technological institutions of research and learning.




4. The tone and wording of the plaintiffs exposition speak for itself as far as profound ignorance of matters not pertaining to foods, drugs and cosmetics such as matters of basic natural science is concerned. I have never permitted this administration, important and valuable as it may be in its field, to delve as an authority in matters of psychiatry, sexual biology, organismic energy functions and the like. This is in no way the domain of this agency. And no authority can be given them in matters they know nothing about.




5. I believe that this is a matter of a conspiracy by people unknown to me to destroy the discovery of the Life Energy by means of disguising the conspiracy as an action of the USA government. Upon receipt of the summons I was not impressed by the stupidity of the complaint, but I was deeply sorrowful at the abuse of the good name of the USA government for such actions, in these times of trial when every single government administrator must watch out a hundred fold not to make a fool of himself.




6. I am not interested in selling Acc [umulator] devices. I do not depend financially upon these devices. Most of them are being built in many lands by people I even do not know and without any royalty payments. Everybody who knows how can build an OR energy accumulator. The discovery of the Life Energy is out of my hands, and it is spread far and wide in many institutions and homes, there is nothing that can stop it any longer. Not even a shot out of the dark night through a window in my home will stop what is inevitably growing toward complete victory over the evils in some pharmaceutic practices.




7. I can wait 500 years for scientists everywhere to study and grasp what primordial Cosmic Energy really represents.




8. I shall offer no proof of the correctness of my discoveries. I insist as a free man in a free world to my right even to be wrong as long as I do not harm anyone. I shall not offer to any court the many testimonials by physicians and lay people alike about the medical efficacy of the OR energy. This is not the issue at all. At issue is, however, the question whether ignorant servants of the people have a right to bother and disturb decent scientific work in basic natural science for many years without rhyme or reason. This is what I shall contest. To permit such actions to take charge of serious scientific work would mean, in the end, to deliver human thought and freely functioning ideas to any drunken hoodlum in any tavern. This cannot be permitted to happen. To prevent this is a duty of every responsible citizen. The right to be wrong is at stake.

To Judge John D. Clifford, Jr.




25 February 1954




Dear Judge Clifford:




I am taking the liberty of transmitting to you my “Response” to the complaint filed by the Food and Drug Administration regarding the Orgone Energy Accumulator. My “Response” summarizes my standpoint as a natural scientist who deals with matters of basic natural law. It is not in my hands to judge the legal aspects of the matter.




My factual position in the case as well as in the world of science of today does not permit me to enter the case against the Food And Drug administration, since such action would, in my mind, imply admission of the authority of this special branch of the government to pass judgment on primordial, pre-atomic cosmic orgone energy.




I, therefore, rest the case in full confidence in your hands.




 




RESPONSE




REGARDING THE REQUEST OF THE FOOD AND DRUG ADMINISTRATION (FDA) TO ENJOIN THE NATURAL SCIENTIFIC ACTIVITIES OF WILHELM REICH, M.D.




In order to clarify the 

factual

 as well as the 

legal

 situation concerning the complaint, we must, from the very beginning, distinguish concrete 

facts

 from 

legal procedure

 to do justice to the facts.




Technically

, legally the US government has filed suit against the natural scientific work of Wilhelm Reich.




Factually

, The FDA is 

not

 “The US Government.” It is merely one of its administrative agencies dealing with Foods, Drugs, and Cosmetics. It is not empowered to deal with 

Basic Natural Law

.




ORGONOMY (see BIBLIOGRAPHY on the HISTORY OF ORGONOMY) is a branch of BASIC NATURAL SCIENCE. Its central object of research is elucidation of the Basic Natural Law.




Now, in order to bring into line the legal procedures with the abovementioned facts, the following is submitted:




The common law structure of the UNITED STATES rests originally on Natural Law. This Natural Law has heretofore been interpreted in various ways of thinking, metaphysically, religiously, mechanistically. It has never, concretely and scientifically, been subjected to natural scientific inquiry based upon a discovery which encompasses the very roots of existence.




The concept of Natural Law as the foundation of a secure way of life, must firmly rest upon the practical concrete functions of LIFE itself. In consequence, a correct life-positive interpretation of Natural Law, the basis of common law, depends on the 

factual

 elucidation of what Life actually is, how it works, what are its basic functional manifestations. From this basic premise derive the claims of natural scientists to a free, unmolested, unimpeded, natural scientific activity in general and in the exploration of the Life Energy in particular.




The complaint of the FDA is factually intimately interconnected with a basic social issue which, at present, is reverberating in the lives of all of us here and abroad.




Abraham Lincoln once said: “What I do say is that no man is good enough to govern another man without that other’s consent. I say this is a leading principle, the sheet anchor of American republicanism.”




At this point, I could easily declare “I refuse to be governed in my basic natural research activities by the Food and Drug Administration.” But exactly here, in this constitutional right of mine, the basic confusion in the interpretation of Natural and Common Law becomes apparent.




There are conspirators around whose aim it is to destroy human happiness and self-government. Is now the right of the conspirator to ravage humanity the same as my right to free, unimpeded inquiry?




It obviously is NOT THE SAME THING. I shall not try to answer this basic dilemma of American society at the present. I shall only open an approach to this legal and factual dilemma. It has a lot to do with the position of the complaint, trying to enjoin the experimental and theoretical functions of Life in its emotional, educational, social, economic, intellectual and medical implications.




According to Natural, and in consequence, American Common Law, no one, no matter who he is, has the power or legal right to enjoin:







The study and observation of natural phenomena including Life within and without man;




The communication to others of knowledge of these natural phenomena so rich in the manifestations of an existent, concrete, cosmic Life Energy:




The stir to mate in all living beings, including our maturing adolescents;




The emergence of abstractions and final mathematical formulae concerning the natural life force in the universe, and the right to their dissemination among one’s fellow men;




The handling, use and distribution of instruments of basic research in any field, medical, educational, preventive, physical, biological, and in fields which emerge from such basic activities and which, 

resting on such principles

, must by all means remain free.







Attempts such as branding activities and instruments of such a kind as “adulterated,” in other words as fraud, only characterizes the narrowness of the horizon of the complaint.




No man-made law ever, no matter whether derived from the past or projected into a distant, unforeseeable future, can or should ever be empowered to claim that it is greater than the Natural Law from which it stems and to which it must inevitably return in the eternal rhythm of creation and decline of all things natural. This is valid, no matter whether we speak in terms such as “God,” “Natural Law,” “Cosmic Primordial Force,” “Ether” or “Cosmic Orgone Energy.”




The present critical state of international human affairs requires security and safety from nuisance interferences with efforts toward full, honest, determined clarification of man’s relationship to nature within and without himself: In other words, his relationship to the Law of Nature. It is not permissible, either morally, legally or factually to force a natural scientist to expose his scientific results and methods of basic research in court. This point is accentuated in a world crisis where biopathic men hold in their hands power over ruined, destitute multitudes.




To appear in court as a “

defendant”

 in matters of basic natural research would in itself appear, to say the least, extraordinary. It would require disclosure of evidence in support of the position of the discovery of the Life Energy. Such disclosure, however, would invoke untold complications, and 

possibly national disaster

.




Proof of this can be submitted at any time only to a duly 

authorized

 personality of the US Government in a high, responsible position.




Scientific matters cannot possibly ever be decided upon in court. They can only be clarified by prolonged, faithful bona fide observations in friendly exchange of opinion, never by litigation. The sole purpose of the complaint is to entangle orgonomic basic research in endless, costly legal procedures in la Panmunjon, which will accomplish exactly NOTHING rational or useful to human society.




Inquiry in the realm of Basic Natural Law is 

outside the judicial domain

, of this, or ANY OTHER KIND OF SOCIAL ADMINISTRATION ANYWHERE ON THIS GLOBE, IN ANY LAND, NATION OR REGION.




Man’s right to know, to learn, to inquire, to make bona fide errors, to investigate human emotions must, by all means, be safe, if the word FREEDOM should ever be more than an empty political slogan.




If painstakingly elaborated and published scientific findings over a period of 30 years could not convince this administration, or will not be able to convince any other social administration of the true nature of the discovery of the Life Energy, no litigation in court anywhere will ever help to do so.




I, therefore, submit, in the name of truth and justice, that I shall not appear in court as the “defendant” against a plaintiff who by his mere complaint already has shown his ignorance in matters of natural science. I do so at the risk of being, by mistake, fully enjoined in all my activities. Such an injunction would mean practically exactly nothing at all. My discovery of the Life Energy is today widely known nearly all over the globe, in hundreds of institutions, whether acclaimed or cursed. It can no longer be stopped by anyone, no matter what happens to me.




Orgone Energy Accumulators are “

devices

” designed to concentrate cosmic Orgone Energy, and thus to make it available to further research in medicine, biology and physics, are being built today in many lands, without my knowledge and consent, and even without any royalty payments.




On the basis of these considerations, I submit that the case against Orgonomy be taken out of court completely.




Literature on orgonomic matters is enclosed for further clarification of this issue.

5 April 1954




Mistakes we beginners make in legal battles:




We are frightened. We are confused. We want peace. Somebody else should do it for us. We believe in lawyers, and respect the law where it is mere legalism and business concealed in the cloak of lawfulness. We do not discriminate between fact and law to execute the factual evidence, and we do not distinguish between legalistic and the lawful, in accordance with human living. We tend either to do nothing or to shoot all our arrows at once, if possible, at the mere sound of a footstep in the dark bushes. We are supporting every intention of our enemies by submission or lack of judgment.




That is WE, the experienced physicians and psychiatrists. Imagine now the situation of the little fellow having stolen a piece of bread, who falls victim to the ambition of a young lawyer wishing to prove how well he can serve in court in convicting the victim in order to please the district attorney who wants to make a career.

Basic natural scientific research must remain free of any kind of intrusion by those who are not doing basic research themselves. One must have the right to be wrong.




Testing

 the society one lives in is duty of citizenship. We must test our standing, our rights, our responsibilities, and the environment in which such standing, rights and responsibilities are being exercised. No petty law quibbling can ever replace the right of free men to act according to rational conscience against evil, corrupt government.

12 May 1954




Between 9:40 p.m. and midnight the following happened: McCullough had just projected for me, with Ilse Ollendorff and Peter Reich present, the copy of the televised Cloudbuster showing of March; thereafter we saw again the orgone motor film. We were about to leave the observatory when I suddenly saw one very bright, orange-yellow oval shaped “star” to the NW of the Observatory, some 25 to 30 degrees declination. I did not take any exact bearings.




The object seemed to stand still, but it pulsated and blinked. Then, soon thereafter, I noticed a second object somewhat higher up, and to the south of the first, of the same appearance in size. We observed with binoculars and came to the conclusion that these could not possibly be fixed stars or planets. They blinked while the stars were motionless. They were much larger, and not of circular shape or color. Slowly, but faster than planets would, they sank toward the NW horizon.




We then left the building after closing it up for the night, etc. The building was rarely lighted at night during the past two years except at such occasions as projections, etc. since it is not habitable and can, due to the DOR emergency, be used only a few hours every day. The objects clearly pulsated and moved slightly in various directions. I thought that the lighted Observatory may have aroused the curiosity of some CORE men.




We left the building. Before entering our cars I had the idea to test my assumption that if these were CORE space ships, they would react in some manner to a cloudbuster being pointed at them. My daughter Eva and William Moise at Hancock, Maine had a few days ago reported that they had trained a cloudbuster on a wobbling orange object to the west of them.




We opened all ten pipes and directed them toward the lower bright object. At first there was no reaction. But when I moved the pipes slightly a reaction occurred. 

The bright light dimmed slowly and vanished for a few seconds from sight

. It appeared again, brightening up to the former intensity. But, as I continue to move my machine, it dimmed again staying dark longer this time and returning seemingly with some difficulty to former brightness. Then it dimmed twice more, remaining invisible. In other words it did not reappear in the sky.




This was incontrovertible proof to me that we were dealing with a space ship propelled by cosmic energy.




23 May 1954




I am slowly being carried out from the realm of man’s affairs, including education. It is space and infinity that looms ahead. I fear it, and I’ve done all kinds of things over the past 20 years to avoid its final implications.




To Ola Raknes




27 May 1954




Dear Dr. Raknes:




Upon receipt of your good letter of May 22nd, I sent you a telegram and I wish to add by letter the following:







According to some reliable reports, the Judge had not only 

not

 read my Response and looked at the literature we had sent him, but he had not even read the injunction which he had signed.




You are the first reader of the complaint who hit upon the fact that they do not accuse me actually of anything. It is just by implication and innuendo that they hint at fraud. I do not think that anyone in New York saw this.




Your comparison of this case with that of Galilei is completely correct. However, I did not, as Galilei did, go to court as the defendant against men of bad faith. And I am ready to take the consequences. To me, this case is a test case, an experiment as it were which will answer my question: “Is it really possible that the truth can be trampled down on mere legalistic, tactical, procedural grounds?” By not going to court as the defendant against evil, I said, for the first time, I believe, in the history of science:







 







a) The quest for knowledge as the basis for all existence is supreme, beyond any judicial or governmental domain.




b) It is to demonstrate that it is not possible that any man of bad faith can call a scientist to court as defendant, because he dislikes what this scientist believes to be true.







As I wrote to you, very powerful social forces are against me, but so are also many for me.




I am looking forward to seeing you.




31 May 1954




Observatory seems to return to normal. I was able to stay and work there for many hours, even in bad weather, without discomfort.




I am slowly preparing myself and my environment for orgonometric math work. The old chart and calculations of 10 years ago are coming forth. By correcting, retracing some of the faded numbers I am getting again acquainted with them.




6 June 1954




I wonder how the Judge will decide June 14th on his own former decision. Here is an occasion to show one’s value of structure. It takes more to upset one’s own decision than it takes to upset someone else’s life work. This sounds so banal a truth that I feel embarrassed to mention it. Did the Judge read by now my “Response”? Did he compare the FDA complaint with the factual evidence in the literature? In any case he resumed the case, reinstated something he had considered a closed book. Will procedural compulsion hamstring his knowing the truth?




14 June 1954




The Fifth Annual Meeting of the Wilhelm Reich Foundation was held briefly yesterday with the main goal to keep the WRF suspended for another year until things clear up with the present trustees, who have all formally resigned, still carrying on the job of administration.




According to Dr. Baker, and a confirmation by Mr. Haydon, the lawyers of the FDA have assured the physicians in New York area that they would be unmolested; that no more investigations would be made, that they were only “out after WR” to stop all his activities; that in 

New York the accumulators could be further used in medicine without interference

.




PREPOSTEROUS!




NOW, WHAT NONSENSE IS THIS AGAIN?




Either the orgone accumulator is a fraud, then it is so in Maine, at Orgonon, and in New York and it should be prosecuted. OR, it is NO fraud, then it should be freed from the nuisance interference right away and everywhere.




This kind of dealing is characteristic of bad American deals and OF BAD GOVERNMENT in general. Again the
