Today Haydon has a hearing in Portland before Judge Clifford on the dismissal of the complaint.




WHY in devil’s name don’t they use the truth to fight evil? Why only tactics? I had that problem before me fourty years ago already—It is their twisted structure—This seems to be the final answer.




30 June 1954




WE EXPECT THE COURT DECISION any day now. The 14 days were over on Saturday. Haydon did a good job on his briefs, excepting, I believe, slowly (it is always so slow) my basic position in the case against the criminal conspiracy against orgonomy. With conspiracy I mean the hiddenness, the sneaky procedures, the use of slander, the obvious absence of any honest will to find the truth, the using of court action to defame.




 




The status of this conspiracy did not preclude Reich’s concern over the planet’s growing desertification, or weaken his resolve to understand and reduce it. However, a number of questions would have to be answered before any desert operation could be laid out. One had to know the main direction of the orgone energy flow with respect to ocean shores, the main wind directions, the distribution of precipitation in inches per year, and the character of desert growth and soil. It was also important to ascertain whether government assistance and the cooperation of agricultural departments could be secured and how the entire operation would be financed.




In March 1954, Reich sent Robert McCullough to Yuma, Arizona, on a month-long exploratory trip to observe various phenomena on actual, established deserts that had been recognized theoretically as stages in desert development in Maine, and to determine the effectiveness of a single cloudbuster in such a desert environment and the possibility of DOR removal.




Yuma had been chosen as the research area because of its extreme aridity, proximity to a good stream to draw into, the Colorado River, and a large water surface, the Gulf of California, but the pressure of many planes in the air from a local jet trainer base led him to investigate other sites in Arizona.




In a letter to McCullough written on March 31, Reich said, “Should you be able to establish clearly that DOR clouds can definitely be moved and breezes and clouds can be formed, then you have fulfilled your task, even if no rain has occurred.”




26 July 1954




The decision was reached by the Orgone Institute to proceed with Oranur Weather Control operations in an attempt to check the tendency for desert development which threatens the major portion of the U.S.A. Burning heat, drought, and dryness, caused by DOR Clouds extended over most of the nation with the lower two thirds of the country suffering from severe drought. The emergency was pressing. It was feared that the situation might get out of hand if no measures were taken. This situation dictated the decision by Orgone Institute to proceed.




Notification of the Orgone Institute’s decision to act in this emergency was sent by registered letter to the governors of the following states: New York, New Jersey, Pennsylvania, Missouri, Arkansas, Oklahoma, and Texas.







28 July 1954




Judge Clifford must be in trouble. We expected the lifting of the Injunction already two weeks ago. As a judge, one must not make such a mistake as to issue an injunction without having read it, or knowing what it is all about.




On August 5th books will go out again to the public, according to my order. No accumulators will be shipped in interstate commerce, to keep strictly within the law. Thus no “labeling” can be attached to our literature.




31 July 1954




NO DECISION YET from Portland. The Judge does not seem to know what to do.




To the Board of Trustees of the Wilhelm

 Reich Foundation and Orgone Institute

 Research Laboratories, Inc.




28 August 1954




My dear Colleagues:




I would like to make the following suggestion with regard to possible solution of the apparently stalemated legal situation. I believe that the case of the conspirators against my discovery is practically dead. However, the injunction operates at present on its own force, as it were. Also, any pestilent character may in the future refer to the injunction if he so pleases. The legal tangle should therefore be resolved.




First

: We could test the constitutionality of such an injunction. As you know, it was obtained by the instigators of the conspiracy only through my non-appearance in court. As you also know the acting judge had not even read the text of the injunction before he signed it, according to one report. To some, it would seem worthwhile to test such justice in court by simply breaking the injunction and risk a contempt of court charge. I personally would hesitate to choose this way.




Second

: Someone among you as the total body of the trustees as a group could ask the attorney of the complaint, or the judge himself 

whether the injunction still stands

. The intervening briefs have been filed more than three months ago, and more than two months have passed since Judge Clifford promised the decision. We all feel that the case of the conspirators against us is dead, but the legal situation is not, and such an inquiry could possibly solve the tangle. However, I personally would hesitate to ask the representative of the complaint, who built his case against us on a clear-cut conspirational background, for permission to send out our honest and good literature.




Third

: Possibly the most rational way would be the following to end the deadlock to the satisfaction of all concerned and with the least possible noise making.




A certain date could be determined when all activities presently under injunction could be resumed without asking anyone for permission to do so. However, we would inform the Acting Federal Judge Clifford of the District of Maine of our plan and would give him the opportunity to veto such action. We could set a date until which time we would wait for his answer in case he has any objections. If no answer would be forthcoming at this date, we would assume that no objections were raised to our procedure.




I suggest you consider these three points very carefully to reach a decision as to which would be best worded to break the legalistic deadlock.




To Grethe Hoff




Monday 13 September 1954




My Greta, dear

*

:




Right at this moment, a few hours after my return from Bangor, I feel as if I wanted to be carried away by my deep desire to ascertain 

my own

 right to some happiness, the same right I have so long and so keenly defended for others. I feel unhappy of not being more reckless, as reckless as any other man would be in my place, just asserting myself in what I want: coming home to 

my

 harbor as you put it. To forget all obligations to situations long passed, to duties freely taken upon myself, yet unable freely to drop them as I would love to do at this moment—to take my car, some money, my happiness with me and simply go away, far, very far away, 

with you

. I feel exactly that it would be right, doubtless, and THE THING to do.




It is not my tasks that keep me from doing so; I can do my job anywhere on this planet. It is not lack of decisiveness; I usually obtain what I want. It is not lack of trust in my ability to devote myself anew, to pour my love out once more, to accept the challenge of a new beginning. No. It is, I feel, one thing only that keeps me in check: 

I fear you may become very unhappy living under circumstances as they oppressed my life for so long

. This is the 

true

 obstacle in the way to the fulfillment of the certainty that you were in me for many long years while silence was inner law in my situation as accepted “high priest” of so many devoted men and women.




One does not take a beloved one onto a battered, stormswept ship. One wants her to be safely tucked away on land, the more so since the dangers have increased manyfold, since I am at clearcut war with savage hounds out to kill.




I ask: Could I change the course of my life? Does it not change now on its own from struggling up-hill to enjoying the peak? I think it does.




I read your letters again and again, and I do not trust my senses: That such a sweet being should meet my path once more in my life. I knew it did, of course. But, after many years, it is still not quite real yet, though the two days were beyond any doubt of concrete fulfillment. I jumped once more like the messenger on the wall.

*

 and I made it again. If I could only talk to you now. Should I cause any trouble, please let me know. I shall retire if you so wish. But I refuse to let go of you. You took such lovely hold of me, and the urge to take you to Arizona grows irresistibly. To dare being foolish in full, responsible awareness, what delight that is, though it hurts.




Please let me hear from you, either by letter, or by phone. (239) 7–8 p.m.

To Grethe Hoff




18 November 1954




Grethe, my dear:




I am happy that I can write now to you. The happiness is rather selfish. In my emotional and intellectual loneliness I have always longed for someone who without distortion and structurally immediate, would be capable of listening to what I have to tell. I said before it would be selfish—to the extent that I wish to ask you to regard these letters as my private, personal communications to you, in other words, as confidential. I told you some time ago that the cosmic functions I am dealing with are the same which, in a distorted or dangerous form, appear in the sensations and fantasies also in the hallucinations of schizophrenics. This was the basic reason why a few psychoanalysts who hated my work or feared it tried to destroy me twenty years ago, interpreting my descriptions of the orgonotic streamings as schizophrenic.




Now you know well what I am dealing with today, with material which to a much higher degree frightens the armored Babbitt and forces him to do away with it all, i.e. with the most burning, most crucial problem facing humanity today, a problem which harassed highly responsible top men of the American Air Force for years. Briefly, the DESERT problem which I am devoting myself to, is, as you well know, identical with the menace facing us from outer space. Not only is this beyond any doubt; it is more: I or we are criminally negligent in not pursuing this problem as we should, with vigor, organization, keen, searching spirits and resolution to win this battle which I termed a few weeks ago “The Planetary Valley Forge.” I did not search this task out; it searched me out as it were.




I remembered at this moment with great love and satisfaction that in the beginning of the DOR emergency in early 1951 and 1952 you were the only one at Orgonon who in a simple, matter of fact manner took my urgent warnings about the DOR sickness and the blackening rocks to Health Commissioner Stevens. I never had the slightest feeling that you regarded my communications as even out of the ordinary. Shortly, you were wonderful while I had to fight not only the outer riddles of a new unheard of fact, but also the hatred and the suspicion of insanity which came my way on the part of several of my assistants. Black DOR WITHIN the human organism and black DOR WITHOUT in nature had thus united or merged to make life miserable for years. I am not complaining now in the least. On the contrary I feel proud in having survived the period 1951–52; I am at this very moment tingling with excitement to be able to tell it now to a dear friend. I would do it again if I had to. And I want you to preserve these historic facts for me and for the historians who are bound to come onto this scene and pick them up. You did not know what you promised when I asked whether I could write letters to you on my work here. Now I can tell: you are going to receive, in installments, the history or 

some

 history of the battle at The Planetary Valley Forge. I know you will not shrink away now since you did not shrink away in 1952 from telling an American health commissioner about that “crazy idea” the BLACKENING ROCKS in Maine. Should you feel that you do not wish to receive such material, please, 

DO

 let me know about it, and I shall cease writing to you. Most of the story is unpublishable at present. It would make excellent alibi material in the hands of the haters of my work. However, at present, if nothing changes, my position in the world, including with my foes, is like steel. Nothing can shake it since I hold the key to the Functional Law of Nature in my hands.




Am I too serious, or too solemn? I do not think so. If I could do at this very moment what I wish to do it would be playing tennis, or drinking a good cocktail with you, or having a jolly time with some good friends here, or just playing catch-ball with little friend Peter Reich. (By the way, he hugged me again for the first time in a long while the other day. He had been mad at me for having lost me as a friend for a while). How wonderful it would be if I could transplant you right now 3200 miles to the Southwest onto the veranda where I am writing these lines.




To Grethe Hoff




November 14 1954




Grethe, my dear one:




I was resting after a sleepless night on the observation deck when I was called to the phone. I was excited and happy that you had called. I immediately understood that you had felt what had happened here during the past few days: I had succeeded slightly in detaching myself from you. Not because I do not love you, but because it was so very painful to continuously think about you, feeling you close, wanting you badly in utter frustration, facing the uncertainty of the situation. The next most important thing is to solve your situation and mine, as soon as possible. Here are the facts:




I feel you exaggerate the problem of “uprooting the child.”

*

 It has happened many times with many mothers that they had to change domicile, or that they went on a trip, or infants were carried from place to place. I feel what you really fear is that once you pull out of your present situation there may be no return. Now, if this is so, then the answer is quite clear: if a human situation is not strong enough to withstand a short separation, then it is very problematic, to say the least. Even medically separation is the only remedy, to find out from a distance as it were.




I would suggest that you consider taking a three month vacation with the child, being our guest here, with help in cleaning and kitchen available, ample space for the child to roam around in sunshine and good weather, for you to take a long look at yourself, for us to enjoy your pleasant company. I do not think that anyone sane of mind could have any objection to this. You do not make any final decisions with this step. Nothing is irrevocably pinned down. You would rest and find yourself again. I am certain the boy will gain much more from your easy relaxation than ever from a tensed situation. I am not pleading for myself. I may be on duty away a lot of the time, or I may not. Anything may come about my way.




If you do not mind, I must put in a word for M.S. [Myron Sharaf] He would benefit too from such a situation, finding himself as it were. (Please do not tell him this here.) Your great conscientiousness may have more entangled than solved the situation, paradox as this may sound. To be away always clears the air, and you are not bound in any way if you enjoy a few months in Arizona. Also you avoid having to face the whole of the question at once and under so much pressure. Why not keep things pending freely for any turn for a while? Because you are afraid it might rip you away completely from your present situation? If it does, then what? Then it is in your path, and staying on does not eliminate, it increases the negative pressure. I feel it is far more your sense of obligation and your bad conscience which pins you down. But, Greta dear, you’ve tried so hard for such a long time. You have done more than anyone would have expected you to do.




All this sounds so very diplomatic or round about. Of course I want you to be here as I want nothing else in this world right now. Of course I need you, and you me. But you know well that it would not work out with me if I felt you are still somebody else’s woman. And it may work out differently if you are close here a while and see me living at close range. Anything is possible, nothing is fixed beforehand, eternally. You do not 

have to

 risk your child. You do not have to be my wife right away and forever. If you are mine, basically, you will be mine, no matter how you try to escape it; only with less agony and heartbreak. Maybe this vacation will only be a transition to either back to Boston in early Spring or somewhere else. Certainly it would be better than the present compulsive, damaging, painful, frustrating agony.




In short, what I’m trying to do here now is to relieve some pressure off your chest: You do not have to leave your husband forever, or rob the child of its father. You do not have to do anything, not even to love me.




Now I would love to stop being the older, wiser friend and physician. I would like to be myself again with you:




I love you, Greta. There is no doubt about it. I was miserable for several days and was about to do some foolish things. I warn you. Be prepared to find a monster if you and when you will know me at close range. I can scream in anger, and be rough, inpatient, intolerant, reckless, ruthless, single minded. But also I am, I must confess and many said so, rather charming and lovely—You know, many young women are looking at me the certain way when I enter a restaurant or a shop. I like it, to be frank about it. It warms the inside up. Unfortunately, I am not easy-handed at taking advantage.




It is nearly midnight. Moise and McCullough have just drawn from an object. We were sitting and discussing the terrific task. (How much more would I enjoy it if I had you here right now and forever.) We had already success in observation, and changes in surroundings enough to warrant return home. (Young new moss on granite formerly bare.) But I do not wish to spend the Maine winter alone at Orgonon. Peter and others long for Maine. But the steady sunny warmth here is very pleasant. Your Peter could bake in the sun as much as he pleases.




I must close now. It is midnight.

My dear Dr. Hoff

As you may know, we are here working at a major research project (drawing moisture inland from the ocean into the desert and removing the black clouds which have lately oppressed our continent). We are combining work and rest as well as pleasure and are very happy in our little community.




I suggested to Grethe to let matters develop slowly and organically, to let her future grow as her good sense directs it. She will probably write you more about it herself.

To Gethe Hoff




20 April 1955




My deeply beloved Grethe:




When I left Boston early yesterday morning, I was desperate. I understood both your desire to be on your own, and my fear to go back into that abysmal lonesomeness at Orgonon. I felt that I would not be able to take it after the seven months of good companionship and family life. I dreaded to go back to my eagle’s nest; and I dreaded the feeling to have been abandoned by everyone, and to have to take care of myself. I was miserable all the way home until I entered the lower house and later the observatory. I was, after the numerous contacts with people in the world, overwhelmed by the grandiose, I dare say majestic beauty of Orgonon. The observatory, far from frightening me, gave me instantly the feeling of belonging to an Olympus of Science. I did not feel deadly silence as I had feared, but the discrete hum in a deep forest. My paintings brought me back to myself; and as you know I like myself and being with myself. I feel only dislike for myself when I am forced to meet people 

their

 way.




After having spent several hours in the observatory (which still carries the smell of Oranur) I went to sleep having boiled a soup with some meat in it. And I woke up with the sudden clarity I know so well in creative moments.




My first letter to you already had pointed out the factual obstacle in the way of our love. Your vacillations all through these months were, as I now saw, not due to neurosis but to the severe dilemma in you of wanting to live with me, but not wanting or being able to live OUTSIDE the trap

*

 at Orgonon. These several months had brought me into the trap too and I loved it, such as the Green Lantern

†

. In contrast, eating food cooked by myself seemed preposterous and unbearable. In the face of 20,000 miles of travel, so much of it with you, seemed to make the rich silence at Orgonon unacceptable. Yet, this morning I had transcended this feeling; I knew now that as long as you were attached to the usual way of life you would not stand living at Orgonon; that you would get restless frequently and want “to go to Boston” with all it represents, not so much in reality but in all your dreams, “Harvard,” and “visiting friends” and “being with people,” etc. I do not say this to deprecate it. I want it myself, but not forever. You want and know well my silent tower where my thoughts and my clean emotions are safe, and this is why you love me too, but you do not want it, at present, forever. You are simply not ready for it. And I do not want, because I fear it, to submerge in the usual way. In other words, 

I want to be alone

.




Unless you, my darling, will or can reach the point where the life in the usual sense appears to you as what it really is, and where the desire for living my way becomes a necessity, coming to live at Orgonon for good would be inadvisable. It would kill our love and may even create hatred. It appears thus, that your wish to be on your own was rational, that to go to Oslo is prudent, that to see for yourself, as it were, will help solve the problem of where you really belong.




And how long would that take? There is little doubt about the extraordinary, outside of the trap nature in you. But if it took me 20 years to realize my way, how long would it take you?




I am glad I realized all this. I am happy being back again in my eagle’s nest with its clean air and emotion. I may dip into the trap a few times more, but I know where I belong. I am going to build up Orgonon further, buying the beautiful oak set and much more stuff. I overcame the feeling of not being able to live without the settings of an unhappy humanity. The isolation is not mine; it is all EVERYBODYS.




23 April 1955




I am alone. Being without a beloved woman is hardest of all. Still smarting from the many inflicted injuries. It hurts so badly. At times death would be welcome.




24 April 1955




This loneliness is beautiful, majestic, but sad like mountain peak in the clouds, and I the lover of humans, of women, of gaiety, of good talking together am sitting majestically on top of the peak on the mountain. I am headed for a sad end indeed.




To Gethe Hoff




25 April 1955




Grethe:




After having succeeded last night in detaching myself from you enough to take a final breakup of our love with calmness and the certitude that I shall find another kind of Grethe, it was possible for me to be less absolute, less stiff-necked and to call you this noon again. I wanted to know how you were, how it all affected you; I know better maybe than you what kind of battle you are fighting now with yourself, having been thrown into this basic battle to which I had to submit for three decades. And I was happy to feel at the phone that you were calm, that your conflict was a rational one and as such experienced by you, that you are fighting now for 

YOUR true

 way and not for a marriage only. I was also happy that I succeeded in extricating myself from the to and fro’s of the past months of vacillation, uncertainty, waiting, despairing, putting the flag up and then down again, getting mad and repenting, and so forth, endlessly. Now, it seems, the conflict will be resolved one way or another for you. You will return to where you came from or you will proceed toward a development in you which, in your case, would certainly not be small. Your apparent pettiness at times only reflects your sense of your great potentialities seen in the mirror of fear. I know this from myself well enough.




You see now that all the hesitancies had nothing whatever to do with your marriage, or your child, or “Boston,” or other such things. They were the expression of a NO which is common to all mankind as far as life 

outside the trap

 is concerned, and it hit me specially only because I am the most clear cut exponent, practically, of this life of the mind outside the trap.




I had to detach myself because I have hard work to do, and this tearing and wearing simply could not go on. In a way, I am glad to be alone now to consolidate my great gains in Arizona without major conflicts at home.




If, as I still believe, you were and are my mate, my natural woman, and if you find your way in this direction, the future may harbor the hope of a happy life together without conflict of such dimensions. Most important, as I said, is now that you find 

yourself

 no matter what the outcome, no matter what happens to us.




As far as I am concerned, I believe that my way will lead further and further away from the petty and usual. I see ahead of myself great tasks which will carry me very far. I need a home of course, and I want children, even if in a “home on wheels.” I do not know at present where and when, with whom I shall find it. I had hoped so very much, and reality has to such a great extent realized this hope, that it would be 

you

. But I shall no longer fight for you, or rather, against your “no.” Neither shall I “wait” while you decide. I do not wish to be kept pending, as it were, like a little man on a thread.




But as a friend, as a man who knows you so very well, and as a physician I certainly shall be there for you. The rest must remain quite uncertain.

*




Be yourself, Grethe; I admire your will for truth




To Elsworth F. Baker, M.D.




18 May 1955




Dear Dr. Baker:




Would you be kind enough to transmit the following message to whoever carries the responsibility for your legal action against the FDA.

†

 It should be obvious by now that the issue before the courts of the USA is new in its substance, that the statute books carry no provisions regarding the Emotional Plague. I would like to summarize briefly the true issues coming up before the Supreme Court:




1. Is it legally, morally and factually, if 

truth

 should prevail, any longer permissible that THE MOTIVE of a complaint should be kept out of the proceedings? In case of murder the motive is decisive. So it is, too, in the case of the assault of psychopaths acting and posing as bona fide government agents.




2. If the motive can no longer be overlooked, the question immerges whether it is any longer possible to exclude the 

irrational

 element from the legal procedure. Since the irrationality in human behavior is today acknowledged as powerfully active, it no longer can be excluded from the law, if justice be done.




3. Is it permissible legally and morally that sick individuals, motivated by their own anxieties, very well known to us as physicians from our daily medical practice, should drag what they dislike into court, into a well prepared trap, under the pretext and disguise of bona fide government action?




4. Is it legally and morally excusable that such activity be taken over, even if innocently, by a court of justice, thus putting itself at the disposal of illegally motivated complaints? Is it, further more, admissible that such court action follow the line laid out by political, subversive hoodlums, subversive to a foreign power, in the execution of the task of killing (in the USA) for mere political reasons, a crucial discovery in medicine and natural science?

*




5. Is it true justice to omit the factual situation, to restrict the total issue to procedural, empty legalism, to force the public to believe that a device is 

fraudulent

 in the hands of A, but perfectly legal and not fraudulent in the hands of B, C, D, E, etc.? Is it sound judgment to follow in this screaming contradiction the criminal conspirators who are out to kill only the person WR (“ad personam”)? Is the law to serve the facts, or are the facts to be distorted, falsified, and otherwise distorted to serve empty procedural compulsion?




6. Is it morally and legally permissible that newly discovered facts be subjected to laws written into the statute book 

before

 there existed any knowledge of the nature of the unknown natural phenomena?




7. Has a court of law the right and authority to pass judgment on the validity of bona fide basic research in new territory? Has established opinion the right to decide what is 

new

 basic knowledge? Have established commercial interests the legal and moral right to kill discoveries by subversive, conspirational means?




8. Has a natural scientist the right to refuse to fall prey to such criminal activities on the part of emotionally sick individuals, by not appearing in court and by putting his trust into the judge’s judgment? Or should the killing of scientists and pioneers by evil men continue forever unchallenged, unabated?




These are only a few of the issues before the Supreme Court of the USA, and not only whether interests of a few physicians have been curtailed.




Orgonon, 6 June 1955




This afternoon came up accompanied by Deputy Marshall (William H.) from Maine District, US Court, Portland, a Harris Kenyon and Hyman Hiss alleged bona fide Inspectors of the “Federal Security Agency” (which does not exist any more). The question, whether I have executed the Injunction. I did not accept them since they are conscious or unconscious tools of Moscow spies. I saw only Marshall Doherty and I told him the following:







I have no power whatever to execute the injunction. I have no power to execute what they have dreamed up as alleged fact.




I cannot possibly order publishing houses in England, Argentina, France, etc. who own rights, to burn the books.




I never owned any accumulators, except forty which were sold non-medically.




There is nothing at Orgonon that concerns the FDA

. The books are under the supervision of physicians. I do not own them; I never owned or sold any books.




Several books were published long before the discovery of the Orgone Energy.




The physicians and others are in charge of the medical OR accumulators.




I deny the FDA authority on the Cosmic Orgone Energy. It was discovered long after the Food and Drug act was enacted.




I have not heard and do not possess any document which would invalidate the last document I received, namely the stay of execution of Injunction of January 18th, 1955, signed by Judge Clifford. Neither the agents not the Marshall were in possession of any document or warrant to contradict the stay. I have handed the matter over to Mr. Charles Haydon in New York, the lawyer for the intervening physicians.







Witness:




William Moise




Grethe Hoff




 




On June 17, Inspector Kenyon and another FDA representative made a surprise visit to Orgonon caretaker Tom Ross. A protocol of that visit describes its purpose and effect.




Board of Social Psychiatry

 Protocol




20 June 1955




Orgonon




Rangeley Maine




Wilhelm Reich (WR)—Mr. Ross will you tell about the visit of FDA Inspector Kenyon to you, what happened, the facts, as well as you can so that we may get the truth on paper? Are you willing to do this?




Tom Ross (TR)—Yes. I’m little but I learned a lot, thinking how they 

brainwashed

 me; a little brainwash that can grow big.




 




WR—They frightened you. They had no right.




TR—It dawned on me. I had read stories but had thought nothing of it. Then I felt it my duty to tell you, otherwise I didn’t feel I should go on working for you.




WR—Will you tell what happened?




 




TR—On Friday June 17th, in the evening after dinner when it was nearly dark, a car drove into my place. I heard the car and walked out. There was Kenyon and another FDA fellow, a new fellow, I don’t remember his name.




Kenyon to TR—Can I talk with you a minute?




TR—Sure.




(WR—Did you feel bad at this time?)




(TR—No he seemed like a nice fellow. The moment they came in the fear was not great. I had nothing to fear. I had done nothing against the Injunction. I felt they had their rights.)




(WR—If it comes to a court action we want 

to show what a decent man like you goes through

, 

fears

, 

when a man such as Kenyon acts like this.

)




Kenyon—When were the accumulators and books taken away? TR—I don’t remember exactly. It was sometime when the snow was still on.




(Then they told me the date just when they were taken away.)




Kenyon—Were you instructed by Dr. Reich to let anyone take any books or accumulators away?




TR—To the best of my knowledge I got no instructions.




(WR—I didn’t know myself of it.)




TR—I told Kenyon that Dr. Silvert had taken them away.




(WR—Dr. Silvert took them away as a physician. Neither books nor accumulators belong to WR. They are not his property.)




Kenyon—Being a caretaker why should you let someone come in and take things away?




TR—Dr. Silvert belonged to the institute. I never stopped any of the doctors from doing what they did.




(WR—Were you afraid?)




(TR—I didn’t like it, didn’t like to be connected with it. I’m small. Never encountered anything like it.)




Kenyon—Did Dr. Silvert have a key or did he get it from you?




TR—I can’t be exact, don’t remember. The key is there. All of the doctors know where it is kept. I could have opened the door for him but I don’t remember.




(WR—Did you give him the feeling that you were a criminal?)




(TR—I told him that I had done no harm, hadn’t shipped any accumulators or books.)




Kenyon—How many men were there?




TR—Two besides Dr. Silvert.




Kenyon—Did Dr. Silvert order the men to load the stuff?




TR—I might had answered yes, if so it was a lie, because anybody knows that when a truck comes to move something you don’t order them to put stuff on. They ask where it is and go ahead and load it.




Kenyon—How many accumulators were taken away?




TR—I couldn’t answer that. I don’t know.




Kenyon—How many books were taken away?




TR—I couldn’t say.




(WR—How did you feel about this?)




(TR—I felt alright about it. He seemed like a nice fellow.)




Kenyon—I know when they were taken away. I know when the truck was here, the date, the number of pieces. There were three crates. What would you guess such a crate would weigh?




TR—I guessed. Then Kenyon told me that he knew what they weighed and that it was a good guess.




Kenyon—How many accumulators were there? How many would you say, how many would you guess.




TR—I guessed a number. Kenyon then took out a little slip of paper and looked at it and then told me that I had only missed by a few.




Kenyon—Did you tie up any books?




TR—Yes I tied up some books.




Kenyon—Does Dr. Reich own the books?




TR—No, they belong to the Foundation.




Kenyon—It may be that everybody involved will go to jail.




WR—Why didn’t you report this to me right away? Why did you wait until Sunday morning?




TR—I couldn’t see the brainwashing until Sunday morning. After thinking things over I saw it. They asked for the truth and I gave it to them. Then they showed me that they had the answers already. Kenyon tried to get me to say how any accumulators there were, and they confused me to lie to them. I don’t k now how many accumulators there were. It is 

like reading General Dean’s Story

. 

They asked the same questions

. You read those stories and don’t think about it. They did the same thing as in those stories only I thought of it as being small. After I told him the truth, Kenyon tried to entangle me. If he already knew all of the answers why did he ask me? I feel bad about this in the American Government. Now I feel I don’t have to answer at all to Kenyon.




Tom Ross

 Orgonon, Rangeley, Maine.




Recorded by William Moise, 6/20/55

Rangeley, Maine

Shortly thereafter, on 15 July 1955, the Wilhelm Reich Foundation, Wilhelm Reich, and Michael Silvert were served an order to appear at the U.S. Court House in Portland, Maine, on 26 July 1955, to show cause why they should not be punished for criminal contempt of the decree of injunction. If the defendants denied that they had disobeyed the injunction, a trial date would be set by the court.




To Judge John D. Clifford




23 July 1955




Dear Judge Clifford:




The matter which is pending before your court is of crucial importance. May I ask your permission to address you briefly during the procedure on July 26. I would like to explain, in a few words, why I did not appear before you in March 1954. It would be helpful if you would kindly let me know by asking me whether I had anything to say.




 




STATEMENT TO COURT AND PRESS IN PORTLAND, MAINE USA—ON JULY 26, 1955 AT THE HEARING ON “CONTEMPT OF COURT” CHARGE AGAINST WILHELM REICH, M.D. AND MICHAEL SILVERT, M.D.




All I have done in the past and my do in the future is being dictated by my responsibilities as a scientist, as a physician, and as a responsible citizen. Permit me to rip open a piece of the IRON CURTAIN that hides the issue here. I am pleading “not guilty,” of course. Guilty of contempt of truth and justice are those who have engineered this conflagration on the public scene, guilty of treason are those who have tried to destroy the Discovery of the Life energy.




The question asked most frequently is: 

WHY DID WILHELM REICH NOT APPEAR IN COURT IN MARCH 1954

. to defend his case? I would like to tell now why I did not appear in court:




At first I was ready to go to court although it was perfectly clear from the complaint of the FDA that this was a well-set trap to kill my discovery and to get me into jail as a fraudulent person. The decision not to appear in court was made when a lawyer pointed our to me that TRUTH IS NOT THE PRIME OBJECTIVE IN AMERICAN COURT PROCEDURES. What counts, he said is the process of LITIGATION. The one who litigates better wins. The truth may or may not come forth in these procedures.




The Injunction itself proves the point:







a) It is unconstitutional.




b) As a fantastic product of sick minds it cannot be carried out.




c) It gives an agency which supervises Foods, Drugs, and Cosmetics power over experimental basic scientific research. In looking through the nature of the trap I have of course denied, on principle, to both court and government the right to decide on matters of basic natural research. These matters can never be decided by litigation.







Now, I am by very nature an experimental research man. I like to solve problems and I thrive emotionally on finding truth. When I heard what this lawyer said, my interest in finding out whether his statement was correct far outweighed the risk I took by not appearing in court. Also, at that early phase, though I knew that I was dealing with traitors to Truth and Justice, I was not prepared to meet the malignancy successfully. At that time I could not know that a few months later several hundred traitors would be cleaned out from the department of Health and Welfare of which the FDA is a branch.




In the meantime a great deal has been found out with the result that I, who has discovered the Life Energy practically, am standing here today accused by traitors of contempt of court. This fact seems to prove the statement correct that only procedure and not the truth counts in American courts.




However this is not the end of the story: Having found out the mechanisms by means of which truth and justice can lose out in two courts before four judges, having furthermore succeeded in finding the link to this mechanism to the Political Plague that besets our social life everywhere, I am now ready to proceed in public to expose the traitors who have shaken in honest, hardworking men the belief that truth and justice prevail in courts of justice.




I wish to state here briefly that this case is only one link, though a crucial one, in a chain of events precipitated in the USA and abroad by Moscow. They have changed their methods in a very dangerous manner. While they are talking peace and bargain 

here

, they are busy there in a quite unsuspected place and with the help of frightened common people, to undermine and finally destroy our trust in each other, our confidence in the workings of decency, our hope and our lives. I am looking forward to the opportunity to reveal what I know about this in public. There is much to learn here.




I am proud to have stood my ground so far. What I have done I would do again in a similar situation. No threat of jail can alter here anything. To yield here would mean no less than to abandon Truth to the practices of the “Beria” type hoodlums, no matter whether Russian or American.

Dear Mr. Fisher:




I have given much thought again to the legal situation; I came to the following conclusion, part of which I have communicated to you:







We are clearly not dealing here with bona fide government nor with any bona fide dispute. We are dealing with a disease, called the Emotional Plague based on irrational activities, called legally “conspiracy.”




The present day laws and procedures do not contain any provisions to cope with 

irrational

 activities and motivations. This is the reason why the case was lost in two courts and would lose, 

inevitably

, in any further merely legalistic procedure.




New laws and procedural rules are required to take irrationalism into the framework of court action. It is my duty as a scientist and social pathologist to try to accomplish this task. It can only be accomplished by revealing fully, relentlessly the true SUBSTANCE and the TRUE MOTIVE and BACKGROUND of this case.




There is, regrettably, no one except myself who is familiar with the factual background of this case. Therefore only I can help to pull the truth to the foreground by questioning witnesses and examining witnesses of the opponent. No lawyer, not thoroughly familiar with the 

factual essence of my life and work

 can ever hope to accomplish this. I had hoped that you or Mr. St. Clair

*

 would be interested in learning, as I am trying to do, what can be done in such a case. I still do not understand your refusal to help with procedural rules and leave the factual procedure to me. I hope you will agree with me if and when you witness the actual operation. Mr. Haydon agreed to help me out with the formal element of legal procedure. I also assume, and hope, that the judge will want to hear the truth.







I shall wait with further decisions until the judge makes his decision as to trial by jury. He has now all opportunity to throw out the case on good grounds, including your legal rebuttal which I have read with great interest.




I shall be in touch with you later on. Would you please handle the response to the reply of the alleged bona fide administration? Please do not hesitate to charge for your services. My motive to mention the financial angle at all was from entirely different reasons.

Dr. Reich: Your Honor, I am not a lawyer. I know nothing about law or law procedures. I know very well that you must not drive on the wrong side of the road. I have asked my lawyer to step out of the case for one reason only—not because he is a bad lawyer, he is a very good one—and that reason is the procedure itself, since it is this procedure which killed the truth, and my whole endeavor from the very beginning, February, 1954, was only to get the truth into this Court. You remember, Your Honor, that I sent you a response when I saw the complaint. I knew from my factual point of view that illegal methods have been used to get the complaint in. I have two basic points in my response: (1) 

Lack of Jurisdiction

 anywhere in basic natural science. 

I denied the right to decide what is truth or not truth in basic natural science to both Court and Government

. If we were to permit lawyers or politically minded people to decide what is right in science, then I believe the future of science would go to the dogs. On July 26, 1955 Hearing in Portland District Court, I explained why that is so and why I have to refuse authority on Basic Science to any Government, and 

especially the FDA

. I don’t know how people who deal with drugs, cosmetics, etc. should obtain the right to judge what basically cosmic orgone energy is. The (2) second point I have raised in the response was the fact of 

conspiracy

. I don’t want to talk here about a political conspiracy. I would like to bring in one point here, with your permission. The way I understand the documents which you have sent to me—they contain misrepresentation of facts perpetrated upon your court. There may be a legal ground to bring this matter here if it is important or crucial to the decision whether jurisdiction rests in this Court or not.




(Judge postpones this second point for hearing Nov. 4th, 1955).




With the 

charge of misrepresentation of facts perpetrated

 upon this honorable Court I don’t think I have much more to say. I have only to add a few words which go beyond that. I have been presented to this Court as a crook, as a swindler. I would like to stress the point of fact. (

interrupted by Judge Clifford, who said that WR’s reputation as an outstanding scientist, honored by the profession, etc. was known

). Then I don’t understand this at all. Thank you.




Wilhelm Reich

Dear Judge Sweeney:




Re: Case #5003




I believe I understand the legal jam which my case finds itself. I have given a great deal of thought to the basic nature of the tangle which is constituted on the one hand by the clear-cut fact that I am innocent and could not act differently from what I did. On the other hand, the merely legal procedural formulation binds the jury to find whether or not I have violated the injunction. This I certainly have done, and I am accordingly, legalistically, but not factually guilty.




I have the impression that everybody concerned wishes to dissolve the tangle in a decent truthful way without committing a judicial injustice. Now I believe that this could easily be accomplished by the insertion of one word into the formulation to the jury. I suggest to formulate 

had

 the defendant to violate the injunction instead of 

did

 he violate the injunction. I deeply hope that in the interest of all and everything concerned you will agree to the amendment of the word “

did he

” by “

had he to.

” I am asking for this privilege on the basis of the fact that during pre-trial procedure I had been arraigned on the basis of an error when instead of dismissal 

or

 trial the formulation was dismissal 

and

 trial on October 10, 1955.

To Mr. Taylor, Chief Warden

Dear Mr. Taylor:




During my last interview with you, you told me to submit my petition for Presidential Pardon to you personally for further action. I am ready to submit the petition. In this connection there are a few technical problems which I would like to discuss with you.




1. I am submitting the petition 3 months before parole eligibility date (November 10, 1957). The true reason is this: The nature of my discovery as well as my well known medical and philosophical theories make it quite certain that the parole board, basing its opinions on current social views, would hesitate to grant me parole. The opposition to my factual discovery on the part of dominating commercial and political organizations is overwhelming. To me this fact constitutes 

sufficient reason

 to by-pass rule 7 which requires that, 

as a rule

, parole should have been denied before application for pardon can be made. The fact that quite obviously I am in prison 

unlawfully

 may be added here.




2. I know many people of social standing who agree with my views. However, I had on purpose 

avoided

 keeping contact with the many persons who know and appreciate my work. I felt they should not be involved in my so complicated case which is related to espionage. Now: Is it feasible that the warden and perhaps the Chaplain should endorse my application for pardon. I am informed that the warden has even the power to 

set a prisoner free

 within his own powers.




To me, it would appear hopeless to discuss these matters with lawyers.




May I ask you for an interview to fill in these 

technical

 gaps?




Sincerely,

 Wilhelm Reich

To William Steig




16 September 1957




My dear Steig:




Aurora just informed me that you need some clarification on Legal Matters, and wish to have ½ hour to 1 hour time to visit. There is the possibility to obtain permission from the warden, Mr. Taylor, to visit me outside my regular visiting time (only 3 hours per month): Call Warden Taylor and tell him some of the confusion that exists regarding our lawyer St. Lewis whether it would be possible to obtain extra time up to 1 hour for you to discuss Legal Fund matters. The warden, who is very correct and understanding, may well feel it justified to grant such permission of extra visiting time. Possibly also, you could obtain such extra time by asking St. Lewis to arrange for your extra visit. I fear that Kari would not obtain permission since she is not listed as either correspondent or visitor. I may only see family approved by warden and approved, listed visitors. Please, have your problem precisely organized for discussion. Am informed that my Petition for Pardon was sent off. I expect message from you soon. Best regards also to Kari.




 




William Steig was granted permission to visit Reich, and they met a few weeks later, in a guarded prison room. Steig found Reich to be very much himself. He didn’t look resigned or uneasy, but treated Steig as a guest, reassuring him, trying to make him feel comfortable. “Don’t be uneasy,” he said. “Relax, smoke, feel comfortable.”




Sitting quietly with Steig, who felt himself inadequate because there was nothing he could do to get Reich out of prison, Reich spoke of his life in prison and raised questions about Aurora Karrer, who was his principal contact with the outside world. He voiced respect for the prison population and told Steig that he attended services and prayed. When people who had helped to get him into prison were mentioned, he expressed only pity. He felt sorry for them. They were “sick, unhappy people.”




Reich’s plans for the future did not include many people, Steig learned. “He would be more by himself. He would go the solitary way.”




 




Undated




Premonition




I hope from the depth of my heart one day in the far future to look backward upon my past life with contentment and gratitude to the fortune which had endowed me with the power of accomplishment and the devotion of service to mankind. To have felt and known the children of mankind as a searcher for their happiness in decent toiling will be the great comfort of my last breath. To have escaped the pitfalls of petty revenge for their smallness will mean a great deal at the end of it all.




To have fully understood what the human race had embodied in the idea of God, to have lived it and yet not to have fallen prey to its unrealities will add to the great consolation.




To have discovered the force of life humbles the highest aspirations, renders modest all zest of search and thought.




In music and in rhyme, in colour and in thought, we human children have striven for perfection which always had only meant returning to the great ocean of all being.




To have lost and found again one’s soul in the embrace of loving, to have spent happiness and to have lived fully the great oneness in beloved mates soothes the return to the eternally fruitful.




To have created lovely children, to have lived their first grasping, laughing, walking, singing—meant to have known THE GREAT LORD, to have felt his magnificent manifestation.




To have held the thread of one’s life in one’s hands, to have adhered to it from the beginning through every single day of labor and existence.




To have remembered every single happening, disaster and delight, in one great streaming of living—, what more can or does one expect?




Endless is the view on high mountain ranges




Unlimited on their peaks the great longing




Unknown, yet close to one’s blood is the infinity of future possibilities, reborn in every child in every forlorn hut. Once no more feared but caressingly protected, this infinity will make Man gather himself into that great effort, the great beginning, from which small souls at present are shrinking away, drowning in foggy lostness.




 




On the morning of 3 November 1957, seven days before he would have been eligible for parole, Wilhelm Reich was found dead in his prison cell. The coroner’s report listed myocardial insufficiency due to calcific aortic stenosis as the cause of death. But, years later a small child visiting the museum at Orgonon would exclaim, “I think he died of a broken heart.”

ORGONE ENERGY EMERGENCY BULLETIN

 

NUMBER 1

 DECEMBER, 1950




ORANUR PROJECT




 




THE ORGONOMIC ANTI-NUCLEAR RADIATION PROJECT




(ORANUR)




By




WILHELM REICH







THE WILHELM REICH FOUNDATION




ORGONON, RANGELEY, MAINE, U.S.A.




 




The approach to the project of experimentation with nuclear radiation effects required clear definition of the pathological functions in 

radiation sickness

 which could be linked up with similar or identical lesions in general pathology which had already been made accessible to orgone energy treatment.




Abrasions, lacerations, and burns are 

not

 specific nuclear radiation effects. They could be regarded as belonging to general pathology, known to be accessible to orgone treatment by means of local orgone energy application.




The real problem was the 

specific radiation sickness

 consisting of deterioration and degeneration of blood tissues, of hemorrhages due to inner lesions, of decay of the blood cell system, loss of hair, weight, general decline of biological vigor, and final death. Would these specific effects of nuclear radiation be accessible to orgone energy treatment?




The anti-nuclear radiation research project had to concentrate on this problem. It could be divided into three major groups:




1. 

Is it possible to establish a certain degree of

 IMMUNITY, 

as it were, against nuclear radiation effects?




In order to answer this question, one group of mice is to be kept irradiated 

prophylactically

 with orgone energy over a period of several weeks. Then half of this group is to be injected with radioactive material in half lethal and the other half with lethal doses. The actual result would answer the question whether 

preventive

 orgone energy treatment had any chance at all, and if so, 

to what extent

 the preventative treatment would be effective. It was assumed that it would not be too complicated to draw conclusions regarding human beings from the results achieved in mice.




The outlook on the possibilities of partial immunization of the population against atomic energy effects well in advance of actual warfare and atomic bombing thus seemed promising: It is entirely reasonable to assume that highly charged biosystems would at least offer greater resistance to the degenerative process caused by nuclear radiation. Details could easily be elaborated with the necessary equipment and personnel.




2. 

Is it at all possible to

 STOP, 

to undo, or to cure nuclear radiation effects without prior immunization

?




In order to answer this question, a large group of healthy mice should be injected with a half-lethal dose of nuclear radiation material. One half of this group should be treated with orgone energy by means of the accumulator, the treatment beginning soon after the injection of the radioactive material. This would be the model of the assumed situation of a group in the population just having been affected by half-lethal nuclear radiation in the vicinity of where an atomic bomb had been dropped. It is further assumed that this group of people had not suffered any direct burns or other wounds. It would fall under the class of victims which develops the radiation sickness during the weeks following the blast.




The effective dosage of orgone energy is to be worked out by either doubling and redoubling the time of orgonotic irradiation or by doubling and redoubling the strength of the accumulator or both.




 




In order to comprehend fully the way in which orgone energy affects nuclear radiation sickness in the half-lethal realm, the mice which were injected accordingly would have to be dissected and carefully examined singly, both in treated and in the non-treated half. By comparison of treated and untreated sick mice, it could be established if at all and to what extent, particularly 

in what way

, nuclear radiation effects the tissues and the blood, and to what extent these effects are reversible by means of application of bio-energy (= orgone energy).




Here, the bridge connecting other degenerative processes with degeneration of tissues and functions due to nuclear radiation could be established. Such a bridge actually exists and is found to be most valuable in the approach to radiation sickness. The latter, according to the reports so far available, mainly consists in 

loss of bio-energy

, in a rapid lowering of the energy metabolism in the organism. The nausea, the bleeding of inner organs, the loss of hair, the anemia, etc. are secondary results of the primal noxa which, in the light of orgonomic research, is loss of bio-energy. From this it follows that charging of the organism with bio-energy contains the great hope, beyond its healing qualities, of REPLACING THE LOST BIO-ENERGY AND THUS OF STRENGHTENING THE RESISTANCE TO FURTHER DEGENERATION OF LIFE FUNCTIONS. Timing of curative irradiation with orgone energy, amount of energy to be applied, number of layers of accumulators necessary, are matters of research easy to accomplish once the basic question has been answered.




In order to obtain reliable preventive and curative results in the realm of 

lethal

 affliction with radiation sickness, it is indispensible to establish the 

kind

 of degeneration in tissues and blood. In this realm medical orgonomy is already well equipped, due to 15 years of experimentation with degenerative processes in the cancer biopathy and other diseases. It is highly probable that radiation sickness does not basically differ from other diseases where degeneration of tissue and blood is involved. Only the 

cause

 of the degenerative process is different from other diseases, not the process itself, except in regard to the rapidity of the decline.




We know from ample, experimental observation that tissue decay due to Xray radiation yields, though not easily, to orgone energy treatment. Deep burns due to Xray heal out, often 

completely

. It is therefore not precluded that nuclear radiation decay will yield too.




The basic mechanism of this healing process consists in blood pouring into the diseased region, in rejuvenation of the still healthy tissue in the surrounding area, in sequestration and elimination of the dead tissue and its replacement by new granulating tissue.




All tissue degeneration so far studied takes the route of development of T-bodies, i.e., bions with little orgone energy, from the degenerating tissues. This 

“T-process”

 rules the degenerative processes in cancer, and also, as we now find, to an even higher degree in leukemia. It is to be expected that it is also at work in the radiation sickness. It is impossible at this time to predict how the experimenting will have to be carried on in order to answer this question practically; but once the T-character of radiation sickness is established, we shall travel in well-known territory. To teach the new techniques of T-cultivation and T-observation to physicians and technicians will then be comparatively easy.




3. 

Where is the borderline, if any, of the efficacy of orgone energy irradiation in lethal cases of radiation sickness

?




This most vital question cannot be answered before concrete information has been obtained with regard to questions 1 and 2. It will obtain its proper answer in due time, and, so we hope, with as few victims of our ignorance as possible. To reduce unnecessary dying from lethal radiation sickness it will be most important to develop point 1, the 

preventive

 part of the total job, as fully and as efficiently as possible.




ORGONE ENERGY TODAY IS THE ONLY KNOWN MEDICAL TOOL ABLE TO COPE WITH DEGENERATIVE processes.




A further great possibility consists in constructing 

bomb shelters

 in such a manner that they actually function as orgone energy accumulators thus accomplishing a double effect: first, keeping the people 

inside

 charged, and second, reflecting nuclear radiation to the 

outside

.







ORGANIZATION OF THE PILOT RESEARCH PROJECT.




There are the following facilities available for the ORANUR project which can easily be extended without delay:




1. 280 acres of land at Orgonon, Rangeley, Me., partially wooded, partially meadows, suitable as building sites, self-sufficient in fuel material and food supply, 1700 and 1800 ft. above sea level, in dry climate most suitable for research in cosmic orgone energy; 40 miles from the nearest railway station, 80 to 130 miles from the nearest major city, with good roads available.




2. Two large buildings, worth together approximately $80,000, one built from rock and cement with partial steel structure, both fully equipped for research; two smaller buildings equipped for living.




3. Lakeshore of approximately 600 yards, suitable for landing of seaplanes in emergencies. Road put in from lake to main road.




4. Instruments and other research equipment worth altogether some $30,000 to $40,000, high power microscopes, Geiger counters, orgonotic darkrooms, photographic darkrooms, electroscopes, microphotographic equipment, etc. Part of it owned by the Wilhelm Reich Foundation, part owned privately by Wilhelm Reich, all of it at the disposal of the ORANUR project.




5. A workshop suitable for the establishment of a small pioneering construction plant.




6. Small truck, station wagon and tractor with equipment for farming.




7. Total available assets worth approximately $200.000.




8. 350 orgone energy accumulators for research purposes.




9. Staff organized to do essential central job, functioning as a well-trained nucleus, consisting of some two dozen specialized workers, about a dozen orgonomic physicians, one zoologist, one public relations officer, two well-trained social workers, two administrators, two maintenance men, all fully devoted.




10. A loosely organized but highly interested fringe of scientific, medical, educational, and other workers on the West Coast, in the Middle West, in New York, Montreal, England, Scandinavia, South America, etc.




11. A fully organized and registered Press, the Orgone Institute Press, equipped to handle all publication matters and capable of rapid growth, with connections through mailing lists all over the world. 

The USSR has ordered orgonomic literature, and a patient of Dr. Hoppe (an orgonomic co-worker, in Israel) reported that she has used an orgone energy accumulator in a Russian hospital.

 We wish to warn against the intention of the red fascists to use the benefits of orgone energy while trying to keep the same benefits from the U.S.A. through slander of orgonomy by their agents in this country. It is to be emphasized that the benefits of the orgone energy accumulator are intended to 

all

 peoples.




12. At present a steady income from contributions for the use of orgone energy accumulators of about $40,000 yearly, and from tuitions, etc. some $10,000 yearly, sufficient to carry the expenses of the job in its present framework. Orgonomic research has so far been completely self-supporting, independent of endowments from either public or private institutions. The present finances available are of course not sufficient to meet fully the needs resulting from the international crisis.




13. Work done regularly at present:







a. Continuous work on the cancer biopathy; courses for physicians and biologists in orgonomic cancer research;

j. Preparation of the orgonomic anti-nuclear radiation project;

l. Guidance in scientific matters on an international scale.







One should not raise false hopes where there is no hope. But where such great hope exists, it should in such emergencies as the present be pursued with all the vigor and determination available. Once the basic possibility is given, it is only a matter of equipment and skill as well as organization to cope with disaster. The few circles, powerful as they may be, which are economically interested in suppressing the dangerous competition of orgonomic medicine, will, so we hope, step aside modestly and decently, and will not try or dare to disturb or even to prevent this overall important task, as they have tried to do in the past. There would be no excuse for such procedure due to pecuniary interests when millions of human lives are involved. We know there are such sharks in the world, but even sharks, we believe, have hearts and some degree of consideration. So do not try to smear this great effort. It will only help the murderous enemy of life.




Let us not fail to prepare in time against the disaster which threatens all of us. Let us give full and continuous information to 

all

 peoples in the world threatened by atomic warfare. There is at present no more sacred duty than this one, not only for physicians, but also for military men, if they truly prosecute the saving of life and freedom. Those who will obstruct or try to prevent this job from fulfillment will show up clearly as the true enemies of mankind, without employment of secret police, political denunciation, or rigmarole. PREVENTION OF RADIATION SICKNESS AND DEATH is the watchword for every decent physician and health administrator from now onward. The sooner this realization dawns upon the responsible circles in the U.S.A and abroad the better, the fewer victims will there be. WHO WILL DARE TO STAND UP AGAINST IT?




The hour is at hand to prove one’s contentions and ideals by deed beyond words. Let us not miss this heart-searching task. Let us not for a second forget that the eyes of all the future, yet unborn generations of mankind are upon us, searching our souls.




Decree of Injunction

 Civil Action No. 1056x




Plaintiff having filed a Complaint for Injunction herein to enjoin the defendants and others from further alleged violations of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act; and each defendant having been duly served, on February 10, 1954, with a summons and copy of the Complaint; and no defendant having appeared or answered in person or by representative, although the time therefore has expired; and each defendant having been duly served, on February 26, 1954, with a copy of Requests for Admissions; and no defendant having served any answer to said Requests, although the time therefore has expired; the default of each defendant having been entered herein; and it appearing that the defendants, unless enjoined therefrom, will continue to introduce or cause to be introduced or delivered, or cause to be delivered into interstate commerce orgone energy accumulators, devices within the meaning of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic act, 21 U.S. C. 301 et seq, which are misbranded and adulterated, and in violation of 21 U.S. C 331 (a) and (k); and the Court having been fully advised in the premises;




IT IS HEREBY ORDERED, ADJUDGED, AND DECREED that the defendants, THE WILHELM REICH FOUNDATION, WILHELM REICH, and ILSE OLLENDORFF and each and all of their officers, agents, servants, employees, attorneys, all corporations, associations, and organizations, and all persons in active concert or participation with them or any of them, be, and they hereby are, perpetually enjoined and restrained from doing any of the following acts, directly or indirectly, in violation of Sections 301 (a) or 301 (k) of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (21 U.S.C.C. 301 (a) or (k) with respect to any orgone energy accumulator device, in any style or model, any and all accessories, components or parts thereof or any similar device, in any style or model and any device purported or represented to collect and accumulate the alleged orgone energy:




(1) Introducing or causing to be introduced or delivering or causing to be delivered for introduction into interstate commerce any such article of device which is:




(a) Misbranded within the meaning of Section 502 (a) of the Act (21 U.S.C. 352 (a)) by reason of any representation or suggestion in its labeling which conveys the impression that such article, in any style or model, is an outstanding therapeutic agent, is a preventive of and beneficial for use in any disease or disease condition, is effective in the cure, mitigation, treatment, and prevention of any disease, symptom, or condition; or




(b) Misbranded within the meaning of Section 502 (2) of the Act (21 U.S.C 352 (a)) by reason of any representation or suggestion in its labeling which conveys the impression that the alleged orgone energy exists; or




(c) Misbranded within the meaning of Section 502 (a) of the Act (21 U.S.C. 352 (a)) by reason of any photographic representation or suggestion with a caption, or otherwise, which conveys the impression that such is an actual photograph depicting the alleged orgone energy or an alleged excited orgone energy field; or.




(d) Misbranded within the meaning of Section 502 (a) of the Act (21 U.S.C. 352 (a)) by reason of any other false or misleading representation or suggestion; or




(e) Adulterated within the meaning of Section 501 (c) of the Act (21 U.S.C. 351 (c)) in that (1) its strength differs from or its quality falls below that which it purports or is represented to possess or (2) it purports to collect from the atmosphere and accumulate in said device the alleged orgone energy; or




(2) Doing any act or causing any act to be done with respect to any orgone energy accumulator device while such device is held for sale (including rental, or any other disposition) after shipment in interstate commerce which results in said device becoming misbranded or adulterated in any respect; and




 




IT IS FURTHER ORDERED:




(1) That all orgone energy accumulator devices, and their labeling, which were shipped in interstate commerce and which (a) are on a rental basis, or (b) otherwise owned or controlled by any one of the defendants, or by the defendants, be recalled by the defendants to their place of business at Rangeley, Maine; and




(2) That the devices referred to in (1) immediately above, and their parts, be destroyed by the defendants or, they may be dismantled and the materials from which they were made salvaged after dismantling; and




(3) That the labeling referred to in paragraph (1), just above, except those items for which a specific purchase price was paid by their owners, be destroyed by the defendants; and




(4) That all parts or portions of orgone accumulator devices shipped in interstate commerce and returned to Rangeley, Maine, or elsewhere, and awaiting repair or reshipment be destroyed by the defendants or, they may be dismantled and the materials from which they were made salvaged after dismantling; and




(5) That all copies of the following items of written, printed, or graphic matter, and their covers, if any, which items have constituted labeling of the article of device, and which contain statements and representations pertaining to the existence of orgone energy, its collection by, and accumulation in, orgone energy accumulators, and the use of such alleged orgone energy by employing said accumulators in the cure, mitigation, treatment, and prevention of disease, symptoms and conditions:







The Discovery of the Orgone

 by Wilhelm Reich
